## Other information

### Affiliation

[Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") (secretly)[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Government)

:   "*It is an honor to stand before you, for you represent the freedom and the future of our galaxy. The once-great Republic and Jedi Order have become victims of their own ambitions, and the Supreme Chancellor is no more than a pawn of corporate monopolies. As a people you called out for change, you called out for leadership, and I humbly answered that call. Together we challenged the system. We asked for equality. And how were we met? With war! The Jedi secret army of clones was revealed, and their treachery was far greater than we could have imagined! Countless living beings—these clones the Jedi created—have been sent to their deaths, while we sacrifice mainly droids. Our soldiers of flesh and blood are willing participants! They are your fathers and sons, mothers and daughters, who fight not because they were grown and designed to do so, but because they know in their hearts that they are fighting for a just and noble cause!*"
:   ―Count Dooku[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

The **Confederacy of Independent Systems**, abbreviated to **CIS**, and otherwise known as the **Separatist Alliance**, the **Separatist State**, the **Separatist Confederacy**, the **Separatist coalition**, or simply referred to as the **Separatists**, was a [confederation](/wiki/Confederacy "Confederacy") with limited recognition of outlying [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") that had declared independence from the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and had its [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus") in the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). Secession could be traced back to the [Raxus Address](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address") by former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") of [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno"), from a belief of excessive taxation and corruption within the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), as well as a general feeling of dissatisfaction towards the neglect by the Republic-centric [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds"). Furthermore, the Confederacy was secretly [supported](/wiki/Geonosian_accord "Geonosian accord") by several major [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") corporations which formed the executive [council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council"), while a [parliament](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate") of [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") became its civilian legislature.

Thousands of disgruntled star systems seceded from the Republic and joined together in the newly-created Confederacy of Independent Systems, born from a galaxy-wide secessionist movement orchestrated by the [Count of Serenno](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno "Count of Serenno") Dooku. By 24 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"), it had become a [political crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") which led to escalating tensions between the Republic and the rising Confederacy. Many within the Confederacy, including its senators, had no desire in fighting their adversaries, as they sought to be free of what they saw as the corruption and tyranny of the Republic. The Confederacy was supported by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), led by [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray"); the [Stalgasin hive](/wiki/Stalgasin_hive "Stalgasin hive"), led by [Archduke](/wiki/Archduke "Archduke") [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser"); the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), headed by [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [San Hill](/wiki/San_Hill "San Hill"); the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union"), led by [Foreman](/wiki/Foreman "Foreman") [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor"); the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild"), led by [Presidente](/wiki/Presidente "Presidente") [Shu Mai](/wiki/Shu_Mai "Shu Mai"); the [Corporate Alliance](/wiki/Corporate_Alliance "Corporate Alliance"), led by [Magistrate](/wiki/Magistrate "Magistrate") [Passel Argente](/wiki/Passel_Argente "Passel Argente"); and the [Retail Caucus](/wiki/Retail_Caucus "Retail Caucus"). However, in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"), both governments and their [respective](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military") [military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") forces became enmeshed in the pan-galactic [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the first major conflict in a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"), after the conflict [exploded into being](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") on the Confederacy's first capital world, [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis").

In the following three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of the war, which had raged across the entire galaxy on several fronts, the Confederacy made rapid attempts to cease the Republic's influence. However, unknown to most of the galaxy or either side, the war was orchestrated by the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") as part of a [long-percolating plot](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") to destroy the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), corrupt the Republic from within and transform it into a reincarnated [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire") with himself as its [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor"). As such, Sidious led both the Confederacy through Dooku as his [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master"), and the Republic himself as the public persona of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") Sheev Palpatine.

Additionally, both [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") played a crucial role in establishing [Clone Protocol 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), which was originally requested by the late Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") to the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") in [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY") as part of the clone programming, acting as a safeguard against rogue [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and reducing aggression among [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") by introducing [behavioral modification biochips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") to their [brains](/wiki/Brain "Brain"). However, Sifo-Dyas' former friend Dooku [orchestrated his death](/wiki/Mission_to_Felucia_(Sifo-Dyas) "Mission to Felucia (Sifo-Dyas)") and Sifo-Dyas' project was taken over by the Sith [one year later](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY") after the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"). Instead, protocol 66 made the clones see the Jedi as [traitors](/wiki/Treason "Treason") of the Republic, leading to their imminent [elimination](/wiki/Death "Death") when Sidious would order it. The command would be issued after a [supposed attempt to Palpatine's life at his office](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), in which [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") pledged his allegiance to Darth Sidious and became [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, deceiving both parties in the process.

By the third year of the war, the Confederacy had suffered several major defeats in the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges") as the conflict began to approach its end, while losing many [starships](/wiki/Starship "Starship") in the decisive [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), which also resulted in the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of Dooku. In the [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") following their defeat at [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") was [neutralized](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") on the planet [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), leading to the collapse of the Separatist leadership, and the fighting effectively came to an end.

Following both the [Jedi's demise](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") and [rise of the](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") Nute Gunray and the other surviving leaders gathered on the planet [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") with hopes of securing peace with the newly rising Empire ruled by [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Sheev Palpatine. However, he sent his new apprentice Darth Vader to [wipe out](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") the remaining Separatist leadership and deactivate their [droid army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"). With the end of the Clone Wars, the newly-formed Galactic Empire, as the successor to the Old Republic, [reintegrated](/wiki/Separatist_Reintegration_Day "Separatist Reintegration Day") former Separatists worlds into the Empire. Nonetheless, several [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts") still survived in opposition to Imperial power. Despite the suppression of many of these remnants as Imperial rule solidified and expanded, an idealized view of the Separatist cause persisted during the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") amongst its remaining supporters, with some still holding secessionist tendencies even into the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era").

## History[]

### Early foundations[]

:   "*The Republic is not what it once was.*"
:   ―Senator Palpatine of Naboo on the declining state of the Senate and Republic[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_1-19)

 [![Under the leadership of ineffective Chancellors like Finis Valorum, the Galactic Republic became increasingly corrupt, prompting the rise of secessionist ideologies.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/ZodKneelsBeforeAmidala-TPMHD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111216232628) [![Under the leadership of ineffective Chancellors like Finis Valorum, the Galactic Republic became increasingly corrupt, prompting the rise of secessionist ideologies.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/ZodKneelsBeforeAmidala-TPMHD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20111216232628)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/ZodKneelsBeforeAmidala-TPMHD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111216232628) 

Under the leadership of ineffective Chancellors like Finis Valorum, the Galactic Republic became increasingly corrupt, prompting the rise of secessionist ideologies.

 

For a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"), [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") had been overseen by the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") from the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") in the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds"), and was in turn governed by the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), which was led by an elected [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"). With assistance from the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), who acted as peacekeepers, the Republic and thereby the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") had not endured conflict for an entire millennium. However, the government began to become both weak and corrupt.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Often when anti-Republic groups arose, the Galactic Senate of the Republic would deploy members of the Jedi Order to deal with them, with some like Jedi Master Dooku witnessing the hypocrisy of the Republic in the process.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616173648) [![Often when anti-Republic groups arose, the Galactic Senate of the Republic would deploy members of the Jedi Order to deal with them, with some like Jedi Master Dooku witnessing the hypocrisy of the Republic in the process.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240616173648)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616173648) 

Often when anti-Republic groups arose, the Galactic Senate of the Republic would deploy members of the Jedi Order to deal with them, with some like Jedi Master Dooku witnessing the hypocrisy of the Republic in the process.

 

During this era of peace, heightening [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") tensions arose within the Republic a [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). For example, when a group of [usurpers](/wiki/Halcyon_usurpers "Halcyon usurpers") on the planet [Halcyon](/wiki/Halcyon_(planet) "Halcyon (planet)") became discontent with the world's membership and wanted their world to be able to manage its own affairs. They kidnapped several members of Halcyon's planetary leadership and held them in a remote fortress where they prepared for assault while attempting negotiation with their hostages. Internal negotiations failed and led the Senate to eventually [authorize](/wiki/Mission_to_Halcyon "Mission to Halcyon") the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") Order to intervene on Halcyon as mediators and enforcers if necessary.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) By [28 BBY](/wiki/28_BBY "28 BBY"),[[20]](#cite_note-28_BBY_Date-20) there was a growing number of senators in the Galactic Senate who valued loyalty to the planet they represented over loyalty to the Republic as a whole. These senators argued it was impossible to truly remain objective when discussing the entire galaxy.[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-21)

 [![The Trade Federation's Invasion of Naboo and the Republic's subsequent lack of aide to Naboo exposed the extent of corruption within the Republic's Senate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/InvasionOfNaboo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140411231155) [![The Trade Federation's Invasion of Naboo and the Republic's subsequent lack of aide to Naboo exposed the extent of corruption within the Republic's Senate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/InvasionOfNaboo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140411231155)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/InvasionOfNaboo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140411231155) 

The Trade Federation's Invasion of Naboo and the Republic's subsequent lack of aide to Naboo exposed the extent of corruption within the Republic's Senate.

 

The [Invasion](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") exposed the unwillingness and inability of the Senate to resolve the crisis, which ended only after the [Gungans](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") and [Royal House of Naboo](/wiki/Royal_House_of_Naboo "Royal House of Naboo") united and forcibly [ended](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") the occupation. This lack of action was a result of [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of corrupt and ineffectual governance by the Republic that had became mired in bureaucracy and layers upon layers of increasingly complex legal precedents, treaties, and obligations. The commerce guilds and trading corporations had also become disillusioned after laws were passed that would introduce taxes affecting all significant trade routes, implemented such that they would have the greatest impact on the poorer outlying [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system"). These worlds were often forced into accepting one-sided deals and refused military protection, as the Republic continued to prioritize honoring centuries old agreements predating the admission of outlying planets.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

 [![After leaving the Jedi Order due to the Republic's corruption, Dooku would reclaim his birthright as Count of his homeworld Serreno, using his newfound riches to finance a growing Separatist movement against the Republic, though he himself would eventually become a pawn of the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/CountDookuCorruptedPolitician-AoN.png/revision/latest?cb=20191130053255) [![After leaving the Jedi Order due to the Republic's corruption, Dooku would reclaim his birthright as Count of his homeworld Serreno, using his newfound riches to finance a growing Separatist movement against the Republic, though he himself would eventually become a pawn of the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/CountDookuCorruptedPolitician-AoN.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191130053255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/CountDookuCorruptedPolitician-AoN.png/revision/latest?cb=20191130053255) 

After leaving the Jedi Order due to the Republic's corruption, Dooku would reclaim his birthright as Count of his homeworld Serreno, using his newfound riches to finance a growing Separatist movement against the Republic, though he himself would eventually become a pawn of the Sith.

 

Compounding this, the outlying systems and Rimward trade routes were plagued by pirates, hijackers and slavers. Due to the refusal of the Republic to create a military to police those sectors, the [Judicial Department](/wiki/Judicial_Department "Judicial Department") was completely overwhelmed, and could not adequately protect either the worlds along those trade routes, or the cargo vessels that traversed them. This forced outlying systems to begin creating their own militias to deal with the pirates, with the [Outland Regions Security Force](/wiki/Outland_Regions_Security_Force "Outland Regions Security Force") being foremost among them. Gridlock in the senate grew, as the number of votes needed to pass any type of legislation turned it increasingly into a place where [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") bartered favors, earmarks, and votes for personal power without regard for their constituencies or the greater good of the Republic. Some began to believe that any attempt at change would require radical thinking and extreme actions, leading to discussions of secession from the Republic.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)[[22]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-22)

### Secession from the Republic[]

:   "*I am committed to the idea of a galaxy ruled by an enlightened leader, with laws that apply universally—not one set for the Core Worlds, another for the Outer Rim worlds."  
    "An autocracy, guided by the count of Serenno."  
    "I am ambitious, but not to that degree.*"
:   ―Count Dooku and Governor Wilhuff Tarkin of Eriadu, during their final dinner together before the onset of the Clone Wars[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

 [![A pamphlet for  highlighting Dooku's , by .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/CountDooku-WordsofTruth.png/revision/latest?cb=20170219104918) [![A pamphlet for  highlighting Dooku's , by .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/CountDooku-WordsofTruth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170219104918)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/CountDooku-WordsofTruth.png/revision/latest?cb=20170219104918) 

A pamphlet for [Reena University](/wiki/Reena_University "Reena University") highlighting Dooku's [Independent Movement for Self-Determination](/wiki/Independent_Movement_for_Self-Determination "Independent Movement for Self-Determination"), by [Ansibella Dellu](/wiki/Ansibella_Dellu "Ansibella Dellu").

 

The first declaration of secession could be traced back to the [Raxus Address](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address") delivered by [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"),[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) a former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who had personally witnessed signs of discontent with the Republic and its corruption[[23]](#cite_note-Justice-23)[[24]](#cite_note-Choices-24) before joining the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") in the hope of creating change,[[25]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-25) only to become immersed in the dark side[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and corrupted.,[[26]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-26)[[27]](#cite_note-Ruins_of_War-27) In his address,[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) which he delivered via a commandeered HoloNet-relay station in the [Raxus system](/wiki/Raxus_system "Raxus system"),[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) the [count](/wiki/Count "Count") denounced the Galactic Republic as a futile enterprise that was hopelessly burdened by corruption and favoritism toward the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds"). Following the address, Dooku founded the Confederacy of Independent Systems and began the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis").[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) Some believed he was merely one step ahead of Republic assassins after his speech. The fallen Jedi Master's words of inflammatory rhetoric would find receptive audiences among young intellectuals in [Mid](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") and [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") universities. Both charismatic and exuding confidence, Dooku's message rallied thousands of individuals by recounting decades of experience within the Republic government and publicizing its hypocrisies, corruption and ineffectiveness.[[28]](#cite_note-Propaganda-28)[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

Dooku's rebellious message mesmerized young psyches and spurred them into political activism. As the galactic crisis grew more and more heated, Dooku's appearances grew uncommon, and were announced with much shorter notice, often spurning violence on polarized worlds. Thousands of disgruntled star systems ultimately seceded from the Republic and fully embraced the newly-created Confederacy of Independent Systems' fiery message of resistance. The idea that the Republic was distant, dispassionate, corrupt, and unworthy of membership ultimately marshaled disgruntled systems into a new galactic government. The agrarian world of [Ukio](/wiki/Ukio "Ukio") found itself questioning what value it reciprocated for being the breadbasket of the Core Worlds, and after citing a litany of neglect, senatorial representatives of the [Abrion sector](/wiki/Abrion_sector "Abrion sector") tendered their articles of secession along with other worlds in the galaxy's hinterlands.[[28]](#cite_note-Propaganda-28) The [Hassarian](/wiki/Hassarian "Hassarian") people joined the Confederacy at some point.[[29]](#cite_note-Tales_from_the_Rancor_Pit-29)

 [![With the outbreak of the Separatist Crisis, the CIS would begin creating propaganda against the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022185206) [![With the outbreak of the Separatist Crisis, the CIS would begin creating propaganda against the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20161022185206)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022185206) 

With the outbreak of the Separatist Crisis, the CIS would begin creating propaganda against the Republic.

 

The Confederacy also sought to gain prosperous [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") world of [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu"): with its location at the confluence of the [Hydian Way](/wiki/Hydian_Way "Hydian Way") and [Rimma Trade Route](/wiki/Rimma_Trade_Route "Rimma Trade Route"), Dooku needed Eriadu's allegiance to control the [Greater Seswenna](/wiki/Greater_Seswenna "Greater Seswenna") and effectively collapse the Core back onto itself, undoing millennia of galactic exploration, conquest, and colonization. After negotiations and attending dinners with Eriadu's then-[Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), the attempt to claim Eriadu's loyalty would fail, as Tarkin refused, believing that an ineffective yet unified galaxy was better than a fractured one.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)[[30]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-30) Thanks to Tarkin and several other holdouts, Dooku was unable to have the economic monopoly needed to force the Republic into negotiations.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) As a legislative branch, the Confederacy established a [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate") under Dooku. The Republic, meanwhile, declared it illegal for its officials to hold formal talks with the Confederacy[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) through the [Republic Senate non-communication law](/wiki/Republic_Senate_non-communication_law "Republic Senate non-communication law")[[31]](#cite_note-Collapse_of_the_Republic-31) to avoid making the Confederacy seem legitimate.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1)

 [![Dooku and the Separatist Council prior to the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) [![Dooku and the Separatist Council prior to the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20241019033343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) 

Dooku and the Separatist Council prior to the Clone Wars.

 

With the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") intensifying as more systems pledged loyalty to the Dooku separatist-government across the galaxy, causing uncertainty and fears that the Republic would be split into two, the Senate of the Republic moved towards the passage of the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"), which would establish centralized armed forces to protect the thousand-year-old democracy for the first time. Meanwhile, Dooku had promised the [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") that he would assassinate Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") of Naboo if he signed Dooku's treaty. The Viceroy accepted the offer, and Dooku dispatched [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") to carry out Amidala's assassination.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Count Dooku would contract Jango Fett to assassinate Senator Padmé Amidala in order to carry favor with Nute Gunray of the Trade Federation, though the attempts would fail.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/NabooCruiserGoBoom-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20240219024853) [![Count Dooku would contract Jango Fett to assassinate Senator Padmé Amidala in order to carry favor with Nute Gunray of the Trade Federation, though the attempts would fail.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/NabooCruiserGoBoom-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240219024853)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/NabooCruiserGoBoom-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20240219024853) 

Count Dooku would contract Jango Fett to assassinate Senator Padmé Amidala in order to carry favor with Nute Gunray of the Trade Federation, though the attempts would fail.

 

Despite the failure of Fett's [mission](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala"), Dooku was able to persuade the Trade Federation, the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union"), the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild"), and the [Corporate Alliance](/wiki/Corporate_Alliance "Corporate Alliance") to all sign a [treaty](/wiki/Geonosian_accord "Geonosian accord") on[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) the Confederate capital planet[[8]](#cite_note-UltimateCookbook-8) [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") and join together as the [Executive Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council"). After pursuing Fett to Geonosis, Jedi Knight [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") discovered Dooku's plot, and also learned that it was Gunray who ordered the assassination of Amidala. He was captured shortly thereafter and imprisoned by Dooku, but not before sending a message to the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") relating what he had discovered. Meanwhile, tensions between the Republic and the seccessionist movement peaked after the Republic learned of the size and significance of its army of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid"), motivating the Senate to grant emergency powers to the Supreme Chancellor of the Republic, a position that was then occupied by[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"),[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) the alter ego of [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") Darth Sidious.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![The Jedi would be overwhelmed by the Separatist Droid Army on Geonosis, only to be rescued by the Republic's clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GeonosisJediDieDeflectingShots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180105183725) [![The Jedi would be overwhelmed by the Separatist Droid Army on Geonosis, only to be rescued by the Republic's clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GeonosisJediDieDeflectingShots.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180105183725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GeonosisJediDieDeflectingShots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180105183725) 

The Jedi would be overwhelmed by the Separatist Droid Army on Geonosis, only to be rescued by the Republic's clone army.

 

During the attempted execution of Obi-Wan Kenobi, [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), and Senator Amidala on Geonosis, a team of two hundred Jedi were sent to rescue the trio. The Jedi were attacked by a host of battle droids during the attempt, and were corralled into an arena. With the battle turning against the Jedi, Dooku gave the remaining Jedi forces a chance to lay down their arms, a choice which [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") declined. In the next few moments, several [*Acclamator*-class assault ships](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship") arrived over the arena, and [engaged](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") [droid forces](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") on the planet's surface, starting the deadly Clone Wars.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

### The Clone Wars[]

#### Beginning the war[]

:   "*Day by day,* grow*, the Separatists' numbers do. Their reach extends farther and farther to the Outer Rim.*"  
    "*Power flows in* concentric circles*. Establish a foothold in the* Outer Rim *before moving inward toward the* capital*.*"
:   ―Jedi Masters Yoda and Mace Windu, on the CIS war strategy[[32]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-32)

 [![The Separatist Droid Army during the Battle of Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Homing_Spider_Droid.png/revision/latest?cb=20130719124736) [![The Separatist Droid Army during the Battle of Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Homing_Spider_Droid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130719124736)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Homing_Spider_Droid.png/revision/latest?cb=20130719124736) 

The Separatist Droid Army during the Battle of Geonosis.

 

The arrival of the clones sparked a full-scale battle on Geonosis, with both sides taking heavy losses. Eventually however, the clone army began to gain the upper hand. This forced Poggle to order his soldiers to retreat and hide, but before he joined them, he turned over [plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") to the [Ultimate Weapon](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station")—a secret project he had been contracted to build by the Separatists—to Count Dooku. As the battle raged on, Kenobi and Skywalker caught up to Dooku and tried to prevent his escape by engaging in a lightsaber duel, however they were defeated by Dooku with relative ease. [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") came to their rescue and engaged Dooku in a lightsaber battle. After realizing that he was outmatched by Yoda, Dooku fled Geonosis and the Separatist leadership retreated. Though they had suffered a defeat in battle, the goal of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") had been fulfilled; the Clone Wars had begun.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Throughout the Separatist Crisis, the CIS built up a massive droid army on Geonosis with the support of corporate backers in the Separatist Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/B2sbdGeonosis-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628193021) [![Throughout the Separatist Crisis, the CIS built up a massive droid army on Geonosis with the support of corporate backers in the Separatist Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/B2sbdGeonosis-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200628193021)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/B2sbdGeonosis-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628193021) 

Throughout the Separatist Crisis, the CIS built up a massive droid army on Geonosis with the support of corporate backers in the Separatist Council.

 

Shortly after[[33]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars_(film)-33) the CIS retreated from[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and vacated Geonosis,[[34]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-34) the Separatists began to seize control of the major [hyperspace lanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), separating the Republic from its army,[[33]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars_(film)-33) and expand into the Outer Rim.[[32]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-32) The Separatists also established the planet [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus") as their new capital world.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) The Clone Wars engulfed the galaxy incredibly fast. The speed at which the fighting spread convinced [Dormé](/wiki/Dorm%C3%A9 "Dormé"), a [handmaiden](/wiki/Handmaiden "Handmaiden") to Senator Amidala, that the Confederacy had moved its forces out before the formal beginning of war against the Republic. Per her reasoning, the CIS had every reason to assume the events on Geonosis would be a victory and, thus, spread out its military for a big attack. Whenever the signal to deploy was given, the CIS military would reveal itself and finish the war just as it began.[[35]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-35) Instead, the arrival of the Grand Army of the Republic on Geonosis[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and its deployment across the galaxy complicated matters.[[35]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-35)

 [![The sudden deployment of the clone army in the First Battle of Geonosis would force the CIS to retreat from the planet, though the bulk of their droid army would escape to wreck havoc on the Republic in the ensuing Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/CloneTrooperInfantry-SWL2024update.png/revision/latest?cb=20250512133359) [![The sudden deployment of the clone army in the First Battle of Geonosis would force the CIS to retreat from the planet, though the bulk of their droid army would escape to wreck havoc on the Republic in the ensuing Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/CloneTrooperInfantry-SWL2024update.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250512133359)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/CloneTrooperInfantry-SWL2024update.png/revision/latest?cb=20250512133359) 

The sudden deployment of the clone army in the First Battle of Geonosis would force the CIS to retreat from the planet, though the bulk of their droid army would escape to wreck havoc on the Republic in the ensuing Clone Wars.

 

Jedi Master Windu suspected the Confederacy's expansion into the Rim was part of a march to the Core. To Windu, it was a sign of how power followed in concentric circles: the growing Separatist forces would establish a foothold in the Rim before moving inward, continuing to advance until they reached Coruscant itself.[[32]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-32) Furthermore, Separatist war strategy accounted for the fact that not every battle would be a CIS victory. Instead, the Separatists believed the conflict would become too costly for the Republic at a certain point.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2)

#### Attacks and defenses[]

 [![Immediatly following Geonosis, the galaxy would erupt into war between the CIS and the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CorvairVultures-AORAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210226011022) [![Immediatly following Geonosis, the galaxy would erupt into war between the CIS and the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CorvairVultures-AORAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210226011022)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CorvairVultures-AORAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210226011022) 

Immediatly following Geonosis, the galaxy would erupt into war between the CIS and the Republic.

 

At some point, the Confederacy launched an [attack on Phindar](/wiki/Attack_on_Phindar "Attack on Phindar").[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) [Quermia](/wiki/Quermia "Quermia") remained loyal to the Republic but found itself surrounded by Separatist space, resulting in the Confederacy beginning a harsh [blockade](/wiki/Blockade_of_Quermia "Blockade of Quermia") of the planet.[[36]](#cite_note-Savage_Spirits-36) With the outbreak of hostilities, many worlds either declared openly for the Separatists or declared neutrality, declining to support either side. Some of the neutral worlds banded together into a loose alliance, The [Council of Neutral Systems](/wiki/Council_of_Neutral_Systems "Council of Neutral Systems"),[[37]](#cite_note-TMP-37) which also worked to establish mutual negotiation as an advisory group,[[38]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-38) not a breakaway government.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) Both sides negotiated with the neutral worlds, with the Republic trying to bring worlds back into the fold willingly if they had not declared for the Separatists due to fears that taking action against ostensibly non-hostile worlds would only increase sympathy for the separatist cause.[[33]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars_(film)-33)[[37]](#cite_note-TMP-37)

 [![Armored Assault Tanks advance through Crystal City on Christophsis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Battle_of_Christophsis_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013044729) [![Armored Assault Tanks advance through Crystal City on Christophsis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Battle_of_Christophsis_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20121013044729)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Battle_of_Christophsis_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013044729) 

Armored Assault Tanks advance through Crystal City on Christophsis.

 

The war proceeded on many fronts. A [force](/wiki/Whorm_Loathsom%27s_army "Whorm Loathsom's army") led by [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") and [General](/wiki/General "General") [Whorm Loathsom](/wiki/Whorm_Loathsom "Whorm Loathsom") succeeded in [capturing](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis") [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"). After taking the planet, they targeted a small relief-force led by Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa"),[[39]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-39) but the Confederate occupation was eventually defeated by [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), Skywalker's [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), [Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), and their [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"). Later on [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth") in [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"), the Separatists hatched a plot to deny the Jedi the alliance with the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan") that they so desperately needed and to establish an alliance with the Hutts themselves. Republic forces [attempted](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth") to save [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta "Rotta"), the infant son of [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"), from the Confederacy, who planned to [kill](/wiki/Death "Death") the Huttlet and lay the blame on the Jedi Order. However, Skywalker and Tano effected a rescue of the Huttlet from Teth, and return him to [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"), thus gaining the support of the Hutts for the Republic.[[33]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars_(film)-33)

 [![CIS forces under Wat Tambor swiftly eliminated all Republic forces on Ryloth, leaving the local Twi'lek resistance fighters to fend for themselves until Republic reinforcements could arrive later in the war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Ryloth_Battle_SL.png/revision/latest?cb=20200408042543) [![CIS forces under Wat Tambor swiftly eliminated all Republic forces on Ryloth, leaving the local Twi'lek resistance fighters to fend for themselves until Republic reinforcements could arrive later in the war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Ryloth_Battle_SL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200408042543)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Ryloth_Battle_SL.png/revision/latest?cb=20200408042543) 

CIS forces under Wat Tambor swiftly eliminated all Republic forces on Ryloth, leaving the local Twi'lek resistance fighters to fend for themselves until Republic reinforcements could arrive later in the war.

 

After the annihilation of the Republic [garrison](/wiki/Outer_Rim_garrison "Outer Rim garrison"), [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") was occupied and [blockaded](/wiki/Ryloth_blockade "Ryloth blockade") by the Separatist Droid Army. The army was led by [Emir](/wiki/Emir "Emir") [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor"), who oversaw the occupation from the city of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City"). During the occupation, much of Ryloth was pillaged by the droid army on orders from the Emir. CIS forces were [repeatedly](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth") attacked by a [group](/wiki/Twi%27lek_Resistance "Twi'lek Resistance") of [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") freedom-fighters led by [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla"), but suffered minimal losses. Eventually, the Republic Army assembled a force to liberate the planet, a goal they accomplished after much heavy fighting. The Republic captured Tambor, but his tactical droid escaped with many of the valuables he had looted from the Twi'leks.[[40]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-40)[[41]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-41)

 [![The Malevolence superweapon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Malevolence-TCWIV.png/revision/latest?cb=20221119221606) [![The Malevolence superweapon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Malevolence-TCWIV.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221119221606)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Malevolence-TCWIV.png/revision/latest?cb=20221119221606) 

The *Malevolence* superweapon.

 

However, soon the Confederacy would reveal during the [*Malevolence* Campaign](/wiki/Malevolence_Campaign "Malevolence Campaign")[[42]](#cite_note-Battle_droid-42) its massive new [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") known only as the *[Malevolence](/wiki/Malevolence "Malevolence")*, a [*Subjugator*-class](/wiki/Subjugator-class_heavy_cruiser "Subjugator-class heavy cruiser")[[43]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-43) [heavy cruiser](/wiki/Heavy_cruiser "Heavy cruiser"),[[44]](#cite_note-Databank-44) that was commanded by [Supreme Commander](/wiki/Supreme_Martial_Commander_of_the_Separatist_Droid_Armies "Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies") General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"). It worked by firing a powerful [ion cannon](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon") to disable enemy ships before destroying them with a barrage of more-conventional cannonfire. The ship gained the attention of the Republic after destroying the [fleet](/wiki/Plo_Koon%27s_fleet "Plo Koon's fleet") of Jedi General [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") in the [Battle of Abregado](/wiki/Battle_of_Abregado "Battle of Abregado"). Koon was marooned in an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod"), and rescued by General Skywalker. The Separatist Head of State then ordered Grievous to use the ship to attack an unarmed Republic [medical center](/wiki/Kaliida_Shoals_Medical_Center "Kaliida Shoals Medical Center") near the [Ryndellia system](/wiki/Ryndellia_system "Ryndellia system"). Having been alerted to the impending [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Kaliida_Nebula "Battle of the Kaliida Nebula"), the Republic dispatched a [fleet](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_taskforce "Obi-Wan Kenobi's taskforce") to rescue the medical station. After a fierce fight, the ship was finally destroyed when Skywalker tampered with the ship's navicomputer and crashed it into a nearby [moon](/wiki/Dead_Moon_of_Antar "Dead Moon of Antar").[[45]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-45)[[46]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-46)

 [![The Grand Army of the Republic detonates a prototype Electro-proton bomb on Malastare.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Bomb_on_Malastare_droid_forces.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210233100) [![The Grand Army of the Republic detonates a prototype Electro-proton bomb on Malastare.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Bomb_on_Malastare_droid_forces.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130210233100)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Bomb_on_Malastare_droid_forces.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210233100) 

The Grand Army of the Republic detonates a prototype Electro-proton bomb on Malastare.

 

The Confederacy would attempt to gain [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare"), which was of strategic importance to both the Republic and the Separatist forces, due to the abundance of natural resources on the planet. The Republic was keen to sign a [treaty](/wiki/Treaty_of_Malastare "Treaty of Malastare") with the Malastare leadership – however, their plans were put on hold while the Separatist Droid Army [invaded](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare") the planet. Due to the low number of military forces on the planet, the Republic forces were quickly overwhelmed and, in the face of certain defeat, authorized the use of an experimental [Electro-proton bomb](/wiki/Electro-proton_bomb "Electro-proton bomb"). In the ensuing blast, the [droid army](/wiki/Malastare_droid_army "Malastare droid army") was shut down, and the battle won for the Republic. The leaders of Malastare then proceeded to sign the treaty with the Republic.[[47]](#cite_note-TZB-47) However, a setback occurred when the plan by the InterGalactic Banking Clan and the Separatists to build massive new [droid foundries](/wiki/Droid_factory "Droid factory") on Geonosis was discovered by the Galactic Republic,[[48]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-48) who launched a second major planetary [invasion](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") of Geonosis to shut down the foundries that [Archduke](/wiki/Archduke "Archduke") [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser") had built there.[[49]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-49)

 [![The CIS would covertly regain control of Geonosis in 21 BBY, prompting a second Republic invasion](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/2nd_Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20120901032809) [![The CIS would covertly regain control of Geonosis in 21 BBY, prompting a second Republic invasion](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/2nd_Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120901032809)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/2nd_Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20120901032809) 

The CIS would covertly regain control of Geonosis in 21 BBY, prompting a second Republic invasion

 

After their [discovery](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia "Mission to Cato Neimoidia") on [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"),[[48]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-48) the Republic dispatched a massive detachment of clones to retake Geonosis and stop the production of battle droids. Following a difficult landing, the Republic forces managed to establish a landing zone at [Point Rain](/wiki/Point_Rain "Point Rain") near the factories. The Republic then disabled the factories' [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield"), making way for the rest of the clone troopers to safely land. As Poggle attempted to retake Point Rain, the main droid-foundry was targeted by the Jedi, who launched a major offensive against the factory. Unknown to the Separatists, the main assault was actually a distraction that would enable Padawans Ahsoka Tano and [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee") to infiltrate the foundry and destroy the reactor core, thus blowing the factory up from the inside. Following this victory, the Jedi proceeded to destroy the remaining droid foundries on Geonosis, stopping the Separatist plans. Although the droid foundries had been destroyed, Poggle remained at large for a time,[[49]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-49) until he was captured in the catacombs underneath [Progate Temple](/wiki/Progate_Temple "Progate Temple").[[50]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-50)

#### Setbacks[]

 [![Count Dooku would back the Mandalorian terrorists of Death Watch, hoping to bring the military potential of Mandalore into the CIS](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907215421) [![Count Dooku would back the Mandalorian terrorists of Death Watch, hoping to bring the military potential of Mandalore into the CIS](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120907215421)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907215421) 

Count Dooku would back the Mandalorian terrorists of Death Watch, hoping to bring the military potential of Mandalore into the CIS

 

In order to gain much-needed support for their attempt at taking over [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"), the Death Watch briefly allied themselves with the Confederacy of Independent Systems. Mandalorian [commandos](/wiki/Mandalorian_Supercommando "Mandalorian Supercommando") performed sabotage-missions for the Separatists against Republic targets. One such mission involved a [commando](/wiki/Unidentified_Death_Watch_saboteur "Unidentified Death Watch saboteur") attempting to sabotage a Republic [cruiser](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser") – the Death Watch commando was captured, but rather than surrender and submit to questioning, he committed suicide.[[37]](#cite_note-TMP-37) His actions, in addition to false rumors, led many in the Republic to believe that [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"), the leader of the New Mandalorian government and head of the Council of Neutral Systems, was training a Mandalorian army for the Separatists.[[51]](#cite_note-DoM-51)

 [![After a Death Watch warrior working for the CIS was captured by the Republic, Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi was dispatched by the Jedi Council to investigate, leading to a confrontation with Death Watch's leader, Pre Vizsla.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) [![After a Death Watch warrior working for the CIS was captured by the Republic, Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi was dispatched by the Jedi Council to investigate, leading to a confrontation with Death Watch's leader, Pre Vizsla.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20100130031114)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) 

After a Death Watch warrior working for the CIS was captured by the Republic, Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi was dispatched by the Jedi Council to investigate, leading to a confrontation with Death Watch's leader, Pre Vizsla.

 

The Jedi Council dispatched Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi to Mandalore to meet with Satine and investigate the rumors. At first, the Duchess and her advisers discounted any Mandalorian involvement until Kenobi showed holographic recordings of the Death Watch-saboteur. Having no other choice, she reluctantly revealed rumors of the Death Watch's return. The rumors were later proven when a [Death Watch commando](/wiki/Death_Watch_bomber "Death Watch bomber") [bombed](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Memorial_Shrine "Attack on the Memorial Shrine") the [memorial shrine](/wiki/Peace_Park "Peace Park") in the New Mandalorian capital of [Sundari](/wiki/Sundari "Sundari") before committing [suicide](/wiki/Death "Death") when Kenobi attempted to apprehend him. Left at the bomb-site was a holographic representation of the Death Watch symbol, further highlighting the group's return. During these events the leader of death watch — [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla") — communicated with [Count](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno "Count of Serenno") Dooku who revealed his strategy. He would force the Republic into sending peacekeeping-forces to Mandalore. Dooku hoped this would lead the populace to view the Republic as invaders, and turn to the Death Watch to liberate them.[[51]](#cite_note-DoM-51)

 [![The alliance between Death Watch and the CIS would fall apart due to the actions of Mandalorian Dutchess Satine Kryze and Obi-Wan Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Vizsla-Dooku-argue.png/revision/latest?cb=20221217211746) [![The alliance between Death Watch and the CIS would fall apart due to the actions of Mandalorian Dutchess Satine Kryze and Obi-Wan Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Vizsla-Dooku-argue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221217211746)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Vizsla-Dooku-argue.png/revision/latest?cb=20221217211746) 

The alliance between Death Watch and the CIS would fall apart due to the actions of Mandalorian Dutchess Satine Kryze and Obi-Wan Kenobi.

 

When Satine journeyed to Coruscant, Death Watch made a [second attempt on her life](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Coronet "Skirmish aboard the Coronet"). Mandalore's senator, [Tal Merrik](/wiki/Tal_Merrik "Tal Merrik"), was secretly in league with the Death Watch, and used his senatorial stamp to smuggle several assassin probes aboard the duchess' ship. This attempt failed, and once Satine safely arrived at the galactic capital, the Death Watch reoccupied their base on Concordia as a staging area for their impending invasion of Mandalore. A New Mandalorian scout reported this development to [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Almec](/wiki/Almec "Almec").[[51]](#cite_note-DoM-51)

However, the Prime Minister was not concerned because he believed that the Death Watch would never be able to take Mandalore without the support of the public. Meanwhile, the Republic Senate had decided to send peacekeeping forces to Mandalore after being shown forged evidence of a senior Mandalorian minister begging the Republic to send help. With the help of Kenobi, the Duchess was able to uncover the unedited version of the holorecording. After being shown the new evidence, the Republic Senate revoked its order to send peacekeepers to Mandalore. This shut down Death Watch's plans, and they canceled the planned attack on Mandalore and broke all ties with the Separatists.[[51]](#cite_note-DoM-51)

 [![General Grievous and Dark Acolyte Asajj Ventress, two of Count Dooku's primary enforcers, would launch a joint assault on the Republic's cloning facilities on Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505212856) [![General Grievous and Dark Acolyte Asajj Ventress, two of Count Dooku's primary enforcers, would launch a joint assault on the Republic's cloning facilities on Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130505212856)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/GrievousVentress-KaminoARC.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505212856) 

General Grievous and Dark Acolyte Asajj Ventress, two of Count Dooku's primary enforcers, would launch a joint assault on the Republic's cloning facilities on Kamino.

 

Following the destruction of a Republic monitoring station, the Separatist army, led by General Grievous and Asajj Ventress, begin a daring [invasion](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino") of the cloning world of Kamino. The aim of the campaign was to destroy the Republic cloning factories and thus deny the Republic more troops, turning the war in the Separatists favor. The droid army was to launch an invasion while Asajj Ventress stole the crucial genetic material needed to produce more clones. However, their plan was foiled when Jedi General Anakin Skywalker intercepted Ventress and defeated her following a fierce lightsaber duel. The main droid army was also defeated by the clone troopers.[[52]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-52)

However, the setback did not stop the Trade Federation from [blockading](/wiki/Blockade_of_Pantora "Blockade of Pantora") the [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora") in the [system of the same name](/wiki/Pantora_system "Pantora system"), in an attempt to force them to join the Separatist-alliance. As part of the conspiracy, the daughters of the Pantoran [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [Papanoida](/wiki/Notluwiski_Papanoida "Notluwiski Papanoida") were [kidnapped](/wiki/Kidnapping_of_the_Papanoida_daughters "Kidnapping of the Papanoida daughters") and held hostage on the main ship of the Separatist-blockade. Following a daring rescue by Ahsoka Tano and Pantoran Senator [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi"), the conspiracy was uncovered, and the Trade Federation was forced to remove its blockade.[[53]](#cite_note-Sphere-53)

 [![With the support of Senator Padmé Amidala, CIS Senator Mina Bonteri would successfully push for a peace treaty with the Republic, though Count Dooku would sabotage the peace talks and later cause the assassination of Bonteri herself, allowing the war to continue.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002081123) [![With the support of Senator Padmé Amidala, CIS Senator Mina Bonteri would successfully push for a peace treaty with the Republic, though Count Dooku would sabotage the peace talks and later cause the assassination of Bonteri herself, allowing the war to continue.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002081123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/MinaBonteriSpeaks-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20161002081123) 

With the support of Senator Padmé Amidala, CIS Senator Mina Bonteri would successfully push for a peace treaty with the Republic, though Count Dooku would sabotage the peace talks and later cause the assassination of Bonteri herself, allowing the war to continue.

 

Following a secret meeting between Padmé Amidala and [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri"), the [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate") approved the start of peace talks between the Separatists and the Republic. However, these talks quickly fell apart following a series of plots by Count Dooku to destroy the peace process. Dooku ordered two attacks–the death of Mina Bonteri, and a bombing on the Republic capital of Coruscant. Following these, neither side had any desire to continue the peace-process. This cancelation came despite heated protests from Amidala, who pointed out that the moral responsibility of the war also had to be considered. This led to accusations by some members of the Republic Senate that Amidala had betrayed the Republic.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1)

#### Renewed campaigns[]

:   "*I joined the Separatist cause and accepted modification because the Separatists pledged assistance to my people. But by the end, I believed. I believed in the side that didn't breed soldiers in vats or send* diplomats *to make peace with laser swords. I believed that even if the Republic was little worse than the Confederacy, it held too much power. The galaxy was better off divided.*"
:   ―Soujen Vak-Nhalis[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

 [![Asajj Ventress lead the CIS assault at Sullust.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/BattleOfSullust-VentressAttack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924023832) [![Asajj Ventress lead the CIS assault at Sullust.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/BattleOfSullust-VentressAttack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20110924023832)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/BattleOfSullust-VentressAttack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924023832) 

Asajj Ventress lead the CIS assault at Sullust.

 

The Separatist [fleet](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress%27s_fleet "Asajj Ventress's fleet") began a major [space battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Sullust "Battle of Sullust") against a Republic flotilla over [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"), with Asajj Ventress personally leading the Separatists against the Republic. However, the battle would turn when Dooku was ordered to kill his apprentice by Darth Sidious to prove his loyalty. Dooku ordered Ventress's reinforcements to return in an attempt to end his apprentice's life indirectly. Following the destruction of her command ship, Dooku presumed her to be dead, and ordered the recall of the armada from Sullust.[[54]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-54)

 [![Dooku's new Dark Acolyte, Savage Oppress, would lead CIS force to victory against Republic forces on Devaron.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/OpressHalsey-Devaron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924024426) [![Dooku's new Dark Acolyte, Savage Oppress, would lead CIS force to victory against Republic forces on Devaron.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/OpressHalsey-Devaron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110924024426)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/OpressHalsey-Devaron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924024426) 

Dooku's new Dark Acolyte, Savage Oppress, would lead CIS force to victory against Republic forces on Devaron.

 

Contrary to Dooku's belief, Ventress escaped and survived her ordeal.[[54]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-54) Republic forces were in control of the ancient [Temple of Eedit](/wiki/Temple_of_Eedit "Temple of Eedit") which acted as a front for the Republic's military outpost. In order to gain control of temple, a Separatist Army was sent to attack. The Republic sent two Jedi—Jedi Master Halsey and his Padawan Knox—and several ARF troopers. The Republic troops were able to hold back the Separatist forces and gained the upper hand in the battle. However, in order to test the powers of his new apprentice, [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress"), Dooku sent him to [Devaron](/wiki/Devaron "Devaron") to finish the battle and destroy the Republic forces. Opress mercilessly slaughtered all the clones upon his arrival, including ARF Commander [Trauma](/wiki/Trauma "Trauma"). Finding the two Jedi in front of temple's door, he attacked [Halsey](/wiki/Halsey "Halsey"), and although the [Roonan](/wiki/Roonan "Roonan") fought hard, Opress struck him down. [Knox](/wiki/Knox "Knox"), after witnessing his master's death, attacked his master's killer. However, Opress effortlessly slashed him across the chest, sending him flying into the temple doors, dead. Upon successfully completing his mission, Opress returned to [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno").[[55]](#cite_note-Monster-55)

 [![Republic forces would assault Lola Sayu, location of a fortified CIS prison, in order to rescue Jedi Master Even Piell and acquire coordinates of the Nexus Route.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Battle-of-Lola-Sayu.png/revision/latest?cb=20200421040342) [![Republic forces would assault Lola Sayu, location of a fortified CIS prison, in order to rescue Jedi Master Even Piell and acquire coordinates of the Nexus Route.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Battle-of-Lola-Sayu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200421040342)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Battle-of-Lola-Sayu.png/revision/latest?cb=20200421040342) 

Republic forces would assault Lola Sayu, location of a fortified CIS prison, in order to rescue Jedi Master Even Piell and acquire coordinates of the Nexus Route.

 

Following the capture of Jedi Master [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell"), a highly-trained strike force led by Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker (along with Skywalker's apprentice Ahsoka Tano), attempted to rescue Piell and his command-crew from the [Citadel](/wiki/Citadel "Citadel")–a high-security Separatist prison made specifically for Jedi. The prisoners were of special importance to the Republic because they possessed knowledge of the coordinates for the [Nexus Route](/wiki/Nexus_Route "Nexus Route")—a [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") lane which led directly to both the Republic and Separatist capital worlds. During the escape, Piell was killed but the vital information was passed onto Tano. Following a number of challenges, the team managed to escape the prison with the coordinates and most of the former prisoners.[[56]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-56) Following the defeat of the Republic during the [First Battle of Felucia](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia "First Battle of Felucia"), the Republic army launched a [second invasion](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Felucia "Second Battle of Felucia") attempt. During the invasion the Republic launched a series of major offensives on the planet. In retaliation, General Grievous sent a number of reinforcements to various Separatist outposts on the planet. In response, the Jedi intensified their offensive and managed to gain control of the planet and [system](/wiki/Felucia_system "Felucia system").[[57]](#cite_note-PL-57)

 [![Quarrens allied with the CIS fight hand to hand with Mon Calamari soldiers, who remained loyal to the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022032555) [![Quarrens allied with the CIS fight hand to hand with Mon Calamari soldiers, who remained loyal to the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111022032555)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/SecondBattleOfMonCalamari-WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022032555) 

Quarrens allied with the CIS fight hand to hand with Mon Calamari soldiers, who remained loyal to the Republic.

 

Following the assassination of the previous Mon Calamari king, the [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") [attempted](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala") to seize control of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") with the aid of the Separatists. At the request of [Prince Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char"), the Republic sent an underwater regiment as reinforcements for the Mon Calamari. After a fierce battle, the Quarren and Separatists emerged victorious and enslaved all the Mon Calamari. Not willing to give up on Mon Cala, the Jedi Council sent reinforcements in the form of the [Gungan Grand Army](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army") from Naboo. During the ensuing battle, the Quarren came to the realization that the Separatists were only interested in capturing Mon Cala for themselves. With this in mind, they turned on the Separatist forces and defeated them.[[58]](#cite_note-Prisoners-58)

 [![Conspiring with the CIS, Minister Rish Loo attempted to manipulate the Gungan Grand Army into launching a joint attack on Naboo with General Grievous.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Rish_Loo_on_a_separatist_command_center_on_Naboo.png/revision/latest?cb=20181124034012) [![Conspiring with the CIS, Minister Rish Loo attempted to manipulate the Gungan Grand Army into launching a joint attack on Naboo with General Grievous.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Rish_Loo_on_a_separatist_command_center_on_Naboo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181124034012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Rish_Loo_on_a_separatist_command_center_on_Naboo.png/revision/latest?cb=20181124034012) 

Conspiring with the CIS, Minister Rish Loo attempted to manipulate the Gungan Grand Army into launching a joint attack on Naboo with General Grievous.

 

Dooku later conspired with Grievous and [Minister](/wiki/Minister "Minister") [Rish Loo](/wiki/Rish_Loo "Rish Loo") to launch another [invasion](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Naboo "Skirmish on Naboo") of Naboo, a plot that would involve turning the Gungans against the humans there. Minister Loo began influencing Boss [Lyonie](/wiki/Lyonie "Lyonie") through the use of a necklace. He influenced Lyonie to order an attack on [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed") with the help of the Separatist Alliance. After Anakin Skywalker and [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") removed the necklace, Rish Loo attempted to kill Lyonie. Believing him dead, Loo went to the assembled Gungan Grand Army and told them that Lyonie was dead, ordering them to attack Theed immediately. Jar Jar, however, arrived at the event, posing as Lyonie. He denounced Rish Loo and canceled the order to invade Theed. Rish Loo then fled to his laboratory. Anakin followed Loo, fighting the probe droids sent to stop him. Meanwhile, Grievous and his army landed on Naboo and contacted Jar Jar (who they believed to be Lyonie) to ask why the attack on Theed had been canceled. Jar Jar entered Grievous's lander and attempted to stall the General. Eventually, Grievous figured out that Jar Jar was not Lyonie, and chased the Gungan outside, where he found his entire army deactivated. The Gungan army surrounded Grievous and told him to surrender.[[59]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-59)

 [![After Rish Loo's plot was exposed by Jar Jar Binks, the Gungan Grand Army turned on the CIS, capturing Grievous, though the cyborg general would be freed in a prison transfer shortly afterwords.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/GrievousCaptured-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122162658) [![After Rish Loo's plot was exposed by Jar Jar Binks, the Gungan Grand Army turned on the CIS, capturing Grievous, though the cyborg general would be freed in a prison transfer shortly afterwords.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/GrievousCaptured-SW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121122162658)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/GrievousCaptured-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122162658) 

After Rish Loo's plot was exposed by Jar Jar Binks, the Gungan Grand Army turned on the CIS, capturing Grievous, though the cyborg general would be freed in a prison transfer shortly afterwords.

 

Grievous replied by drawing two lightsabers, and killing several Gungan warriors. His rampage was stopped, however, when General [Roos Tarpals](/wiki/Roos_Tarpals "Roos Tarpals") stabbed him with an electric spear–yet during this heroic act, the cyborg also stabbed Tarpals through the heart, killing him. Just before he died, Tarpals drove his spear all the way through Grievous, allowing the rest of the Gungan warriors to disable Grievous with boombas. At the same time, Skywalker found Dooku's lair, after following Rish Loo to an ancient cliffside-structure. Unknown to Skywalker, the lair was actually a trap set by Count Dooku, designed to capture him. Dooku killed Loo for his incompetence, and following a lightsaber battle, involving Dooku and several [MagnaGuards](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard"), Skywalker was captured and taken hostage. Shortly after Skywalker's capture, Padmé Amidala received a message from Dooku on her holoprojector. During the exchange, Dooku told Amidala that he had captured Skywalker. He then demanded that Amidala give back General Grievous in return for Skywalker. She reluctantly agreed, and the prisoner exchange took place shortly thereafter. Following the prisoner-exchange, the Separatist forces retreated.[[59]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-59)

 [![Umbara's decision to join the CIS would lead to a brutal Republic invasion of the planet, with the Umbarans suffering heavy casualties against the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Stub-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20220514020237) [![Umbara's decision to join the CIS would lead to a brutal Republic invasion of the planet, with the Umbarans suffering heavy casualties against the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Stub-Umbara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220514020237)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Stub-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20220514020237) 

Umbara's decision to join the CIS would lead to a brutal Republic invasion of the planet, with the Umbarans suffering heavy casualties against the Republic.

 

After the assassination of senator [Mee Deechi](/wiki/Mee_Deechi "Mee Deechi") at the hands of [Lolo Purs](/wiki/Lolo_Purs "Lolo Purs"),[[60]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-60) the planet [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara") seceded from the Galactic Republic and joined the Confederacy, pledging the [Umbaran Militia](/wiki/Umbaran_Militia "Umbaran Militia") and its advanced technology to the cause. Because of this action, the Republic launched an [invasion of Umbara](/wiki/Battle_of_Umbara "Battle of Umbara").[[61]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-61) The Umbarans and the Separatists put up heavy resistance against the invaders. Despite their efforts and Jedi General [Pong Krell](/wiki/Pong_Krell "Pong Krell")'s treason against the Republic, Umbara successfully became part of the Republic again.[[62]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-62)

 [![The CIS would forge an alliance with the reemerging Zygerrian Slave Empire to forcefully take control of the planet Kiros, enslaving the local Togruta colonists.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DookuDnarArriveOnKiros-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111201172204) [![The CIS would forge an alliance with the reemerging Zygerrian Slave Empire to forcefully take control of the planet Kiros, enslaving the local Togruta colonists.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DookuDnarArriveOnKiros-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111201172204)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DookuDnarArriveOnKiros-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111201172204) 

The CIS would forge an alliance with the reemerging Zygerrian Slave Empire to forcefully take control of the planet Kiros, enslaving the local Togruta colonists.

 

The Confederacy, meanwhile, had formed an alliance with [Queen Miraj Scintel](/wiki/Miraj_Scintel "Miraj Scintel"), leader of the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire"). As part of the deal, the Confederacy [conquered](/wiki/Conquest_of_Kiros "Conquest of Kiros") a [Togruta](/wiki/Togruta "Togruta") colony on [Kiros](/wiki/Kiros "Kiros") and enslaved all of its inhabitants.[[63]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-63) However, their plans were foiled when the Jedi managed to track the missing colonists to [the Zygerrian homeworld](/wiki/Zygerria "Zygerria").
