The Jedi Council then sent Anakin Skywalker, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Ahsoka Tano to infiltrate the slave markets where the colonists were being held. During their attempted rescue, Kenobi and Skywalker were captured. Kenobi was sent to a [slave-processing facility](/wiki/Kadavo_slave_processing_facility "Kadavo slave processing facility"), while Skywalker became the personal slave of the Queen. While being held as the Queen's slave, Scintel developed feelings for Anakin. When she was ordered by Dooku to kill him, she refused. As a punishment for her defiance, Dooku mortally injured her. Seeing his opportunity, Skywalker freed Tano, and carried the Queen onto a slave-ship, upon which he escaped.[[64]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-64)

 [![Imediantly following their Queen's death at Dooku's hand, Republic forces would assault the Zygerrian's slave processing facility on Kadavo, rescuing the imprisoned Togruta and causing the collapse of their slave empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/CT-4860-Piloting.png/revision/latest?cb=20240705001941) [![Imediantly following their Queen's death at Dooku's hand, Republic forces would assault the Zygerrian's slave processing facility on Kadavo, rescuing the imprisoned Togruta and causing the collapse of their slave empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/CT-4860-Piloting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240705001941)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/CT-4860-Piloting.png/revision/latest?cb=20240705001941) 

Imediantly following their Queen's death at Dooku's hand, Republic forces would assault the Zygerrian's slave processing facility on Kadavo, rescuing the imprisoned Togruta and causing the collapse of their slave empire.

 

Following Skywalker's escape, the Queen, before perishing, revealed to him the location of the processing facility where Kenobi and the missing Togruta-colonists were being held, [Kadavo](/wiki/Kadavo "Kadavo"). Having discovered the location and told the Jedi Council, Skywalker and Tano arrived at the facility. They [attempted to break into the facility](/wiki/Battle_of_Kadavo "Battle of Kadavo") but failed. Soon after their arrival, Republic [reinforcements](/wiki/Plo_Koon%27s_second_fleet "Plo Koon's second fleet") arrived, and the facility's defenses were soon disabled. With no hope of escape, [Keeper](/wiki/Keeper "Keeper") [Agruss](/wiki/Agruss "Agruss") attempted to kill the colonists by dropping them into a volcanic pit. However, his plan was foiled when Tano devised a plan to rescue the colonists, and he was killed. With the successful rescue of Kenobi and the colonists, the Jedi departed the facility, and destroyed it.[[65]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-65)

 [![Senators from both the Republic and CIS met on the neutral planet Mandalore, hoping to once again bring about a peaceful resolution to the war, though the negotiations would fall apart following an incident triggered by Lux Bonteri, Mina Bonteri's son.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211042616) [![Senators from both the Republic and CIS met on the neutral planet Mandalore, hoping to once again bring about a peaceful resolution to the war, though the negotiations would fall apart following an incident triggered by Lux Bonteri, Mina Bonteri's son.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121211042616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211042616) 

Senators from both the Republic and CIS met on the neutral planet Mandalore, hoping to once again bring about a peaceful resolution to the war, though the negotiations would fall apart following an incident triggered by Lux Bonteri, Mina Bonteri's son.

 

At the height of the Clone Wars, the Confederacy of Independent Systems held a peace conference with the Galactic Republic on the neutral planet Mandalore between representatives of both governments in an effort to end the pan-galactic conflict. The conference was presided over by Duchess Satine Kryze within her [royal palace](/wiki/Sundari_Royal_Palace "Sundari Royal Palace") in the [New Mandalorian](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians") capital Sundari. At the beginning of the meeting, Naboo Senator Padmé Amidala opened up the discussions, leading the Republic senators in the peace negotiations, but she was quickly rebuffed by Senator [Voe Atell](/wiki/Voe_Atell "Voe Atell"), who called for the Republic to declare the Separatist-state legitimate. However, before the delegates could further discuss their terms of peace, [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri"), son of the late [Onderonian](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon") senator Mina Bonteri, interrupted the summit, and announced to the politicians that it was Count Dooku that had his mother murdered. This led young Bonteri to soon afterward be escorted out by Separatist commando-droids, allowing the discussion to continue. Shortly after his escape, however, the negotiations fell apart completely, along with hopes of gaining the full legitimacy it sought.[[38]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-38)

 [![The CIS backed Sanjay Rash's coup to become King of Onderon, allowing the planet to fall under CIS control, which was opposed by a local insurrection to reinstate the former King Ramsis Dendup.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/OnderonRoyalGuard-FR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131017193508) [![The CIS backed Sanjay Rash's coup to become King of Onderon, allowing the planet to fall under CIS control, which was opposed by a local insurrection to reinstate the former King Ramsis Dendup.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/OnderonRoyalGuard-FR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131017193508)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/OnderonRoyalGuard-FR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131017193508) 

The CIS backed Sanjay Rash's coup to become King of Onderon, allowing the planet to fall under CIS control, which was opposed by a local insurrection to reinstate the former King Ramsis Dendup.

 

With Onderon's secession from the Galactic Republic at the beginning of the Clone Wars having been instigated[[66]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-66) by a [Separatist coup](/wiki/Invasion_of_Onderon "Invasion of Onderon"),[[67]](#cite_note-TCW-67) King [Sanjay Rash](/wiki/Sanjay_Rash "Sanjay Rash") found his regime, backed by the Confederacy of Independent Systems, challenged by a group of [rebels](/wiki/Onderon_rebels "Onderon rebels") [organized](/wiki/Onderonian_Civil_War "Onderonian Civil War") by the young insurgents [Steela](/wiki/Steela_Gerrera "Steela Gerrera") and [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera"). The rebels hoped to restore the deposed King [Ramsis Dendup](/wiki/Ramsis_Dendup "Ramsis Dendup") to the throne. Seeing an opportunity to engage the Confederacy on another front, the Republic began to fund the rebels with credits and arms to combat Rash's occupational forces from the Separatist Droid Army. The Jedi High Council sent a team of advisors to train the rebels, along with some of the 501st Legion who were covertly inserted into Onderon, and who oversaw training-sessions at the insurgency's jungle camp. Midway through the training, the camp was attacked, and the lessons escalated into actual combat when a battle droid-squadron attempted to exterminate the rebels; however, the newly-trained rebels eliminated the enemy droid-squad.[[66]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-66)

 [![Despite gaining additional battle droids from the CIS, King Rash would lose more of the people's support in favor of the growing insurrection, with even the Royal Guard of Onderon turning against him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Tandin_holds_Rash_at_lance_point_Onderon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170228060039) [![Despite gaining additional battle droids from the CIS, King Rash would lose more of the people's support in favor of the growing insurrection, with even the Royal Guard of Onderon turning against him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Tandin_holds_Rash_at_lance_point_Onderon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170228060039)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Tandin_holds_Rash_at_lance_point_Onderon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170228060039) 

Despite gaining additional battle droids from the CIS, King Rash would lose more of the people's support in favor of the growing insurrection, with even the Royal Guard of Onderon turning against him.

 

The rebels then infiltrated the Separatist-occupied capital [Iziz](/wiki/Iziz "Iziz"), conducting strikes on droid patrols throughout the city. They also targeted Iziz's main power generator to extinguish the battle droids recharging source, and also proving they were capable of challenging the Separatists and Rash. Count Dooku sent King Rash reinforcements under the command of the [super tactical droid](/wiki/ST-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") General [Kalani](/wiki/Kalani "Kalani").[[68]](#cite_note-Front_Runners-68) After the rebels attempted and failed to free the deposed King Dendup, King Rash ordered his public execution. However, his plans were foiled when General Tandin and his royal guards sided with the rebels during Rash's attempted execution of Dendup, helping Gerrera and her insurgents rescue Dendup, He also pledged the [Royal Onderon Militia](/wiki/Royal_Onderon_Militia "Royal Onderon Militia") to their forces.[[69]](#cite_note-Soft_War-69)

 [![CIS forces besiege the insurrectionist's base with HMP droid gunships, desperate to maintain their occupation of the planet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/BattleOfOnderon-TP.png/revision/latest?cb=20131018230017) [![CIS forces besiege the insurrectionist's base with HMP droid gunships, desperate to maintain their occupation of the planet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/BattleOfOnderon-TP.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131018230017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/BattleOfOnderon-TP.png/revision/latest?cb=20131018230017) 

CIS forces besiege the insurrectionist's base with HMP droid gunships, desperate to maintain their occupation of the planet.

 

With Steela appointed by Dendup as their commanding general, the joint rebel and royal soldiers pulled out from Iziz, hoping to preserve civilian lives by isolating armed conflict to the eastern highlands. As full-scale fighting began, the rebels used the mountainous terrain against the Separatists, and despite heavy casualties, won the battle with the help of illegal rocket-launchers supplied to them though underworld contacts. Faced with this catastrophic defeat, Dooku contacted Rash and Kalani. Rash explained what had happened, and that they would need even more help to defeat the rebels. Dooku refused, not wanting another war to deal with. He commanded Kalani to call back all of the droid-forces from the planet, and withdraw to [Agamar](/wiki/Agamar "Agamar"). As Rash angrily protested, Kalani shot the deluded king, killing him.[[70]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-70)

 [![A CIS Super Tactical Droid used a captured Republic star destroyer full of volatile rydonium to nearly destroy a large portion of Republic leadership in the Carida Incident, though the attack would be sabotaged by a single Republic astromech droid, R2-D2.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/RenownBlownToBits-PoNR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024041617) [![A CIS Super Tactical Droid used a captured Republic star destroyer full of volatile rydonium to nearly destroy a large portion of Republic leadership in the Carida Incident, though the attack would be sabotaged by a single Republic astromech droid, R2-D2.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/RenownBlownToBits-PoNR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131024041617)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/RenownBlownToBits-PoNR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024041617) 

A CIS Super Tactical Droid used a captured Republic star destroyer full of volatile rydonium to nearly destroy a large portion of Republic leadership in the Carida Incident, though the attack would be sabotaged by a single Republic astromech droid, R2-D2.

 

The [Carida Incident](/wiki/Carida_Incident "Carida Incident") was the result of a mission undertaken by the Confederacy of Independent Systems who sabotaged the *[Renown](/wiki/Renown "Renown")*, a [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer"), by loading it with rhydonium canisters with the intention of ramming it into the [*Valor* space station](/wiki/Valor_(space_station) "Valor (space station)"), the site of a Republic strategy conference. While [escaping](/wiki/Escape_from_Abafar "Escape from Abafar") [Abafar](/wiki/Abafar "Abafar"), the D-Squad took refuge in the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer"), on which they planned to return the stolen Separatist encryption module, but they discovered it was overrun by droids. They undertook efforts to disrupt the Confederate plot and stop the ship from destroying a [Republic strategy conference](/wiki/Republic_strategy_conference "Republic strategy conference") in the [Carida system](/wiki/Carida_system "Carida system").[[71]](#cite_note-Point_of_No_Return-71)

 [![The CIS would obtain control over the ring world Ringo Vinda, resulting in a Republic invasion of the planet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/RingoVindaBattle-TU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226065502) [![The CIS would obtain control over the ring world Ringo Vinda, resulting in a Republic invasion of the planet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/RingoVindaBattle-TU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200226065502)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/RingoVindaBattle-TU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226065502) 

The CIS would obtain control over the ring world Ringo Vinda, resulting in a Republic invasion of the planet.

 

The [Battle of Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda "Battle of Ringo Vinda") took place outside a [Separatist-controlled space station](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda_space_station "Ringo Vinda space station") that surrounded the planet of [Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda "Ringo Vinda"). Initially the battle was moving in the favor of the Republic. However, the battle turned in the Separatists favor when a clone trooper, [Tup](/wiki/Tup "Tup"), malfunctioned and executed [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") early, killing Jedi General [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar"). With their momentum lost, the Republic had no option other than to withdraw. The unusual behavior of the Republic was noticed by Separatist [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Trench](/wiki/Trench "Trench") who reported it to Dooku, who then reported it to Darth Sidious. Sidious ordered the capture of the clone, which the Separatists successfully undertook before the Republic left Ringo Vinda. However, before Tup could be delivered to the Confederacy for study, he was recaptured by Anakin Skywalker and the Republic on the [ongoing](/wiki/Kraken%27s_Maxillipede_shuttle "Kraken's Maxillipede shuttle") [shuttle](/wiki/Maxillipede_shuttle "Maxillipede shuttle"), with [Kraken](/wiki/Kraken "Kraken") killed in the raid, and made it to Kamino.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-72)

 [![CIS forces under Dooku's direct command would launch a brutal invasion of the Banking Clan capital on Scipio.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/DiplomaticCorps-CotH.png/revision/latest?cb=20190423144845) [![CIS forces under Dooku's direct command would launch a brutal invasion of the Banking Clan capital on Scipio.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/DiplomaticCorps-CotH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190423144845)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/DiplomaticCorps-CotH.png/revision/latest?cb=20190423144845) 

CIS forces under Dooku's direct command would launch a brutal invasion of the Banking Clan capital on Scipio.

 

Meanwhile, one the Confederacy's backers, the Banking Clan, which was previously deregulated, was on the verge of collapse. The [Core Five](/wiki/Core_Five "Core Five") were embezzling the funds needed for both sides, but Padmé and Clovis, who narrowly escaped the bounty hunter [Embo](/wiki/Embo "Embo") on the planet of [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio"), presented the evidence of their embezzlements and Clovis became the new head of the Banking Clan.[[73]](#cite_note-TRoC-73) While Clovis worked to get the banks back to neutrality after Padmé and Separatist Senator [Bec Lawise](/wiki/Bec_Lawise "Bec Lawise") oversaw the transfer of power, Dooku had Clovis raise the Republic's interest rates, but leave the Separatist's rates untouched, despite his objections. The droid army, led by Dooku and a rebuilt Kraken, descended onto Scipio, invading the planet and defeated the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard") led by Commander [Thorn](/wiki/Thorn "Thorn"). Dooku proposed arresting Padmé, but Bec Lawise objected, stating the Separatist Senate would not allow for it, earning him a blast for his objections, and removing another Separatist Senator from the government.[[74]](#cite_note-Crisis_Heart-74)

 [![Faced with a Republic counterattack, Dooku's forces would retreat from Scipio, causing the Banking Clan to fall under control of the Supreme Chancellor of the Republic, who was secretly Dooku's Sith master, Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/BattleOfScipio-CatH.png/revision/latest?cb=20150410062545) [![Faced with a Republic counterattack, Dooku's forces would retreat from Scipio, causing the Banking Clan to fall under control of the Supreme Chancellor of the Republic, who was secretly Dooku's Sith master, Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/BattleOfScipio-CatH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150410062545)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/BattleOfScipio-CatH.png/revision/latest?cb=20150410062545) 

Faced with a Republic counterattack, Dooku's forces would retreat from Scipio, causing the Banking Clan to fall under control of the Supreme Chancellor of the Republic, who was secretly Dooku's Sith master, Darth Sidious.

 

Eventually, Republic forces led by General Skywalker came to Scipio to free the planet and Padmé, while Dooku and Kraken left the fighting to the remaining forces. The Republic won the battle, at the cost of Clovis's death, which allowed the Banking Clan to be placed under Palpatine, with the Republic no longer having to go bankrupt.[[74]](#cite_note-Crisis_Heart-74) However, a faction of the banks led by San Hill remained,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) while the Separatists could no longer get the loans from the main faction.[[74]](#cite_note-Crisis_Heart-74)

 [![After Count Dooku carried out a genocide on Mahranee, the Jedi Council would dispatch Jedi Master Quinlan Voss alongside Dooku's former acolyte, Asajj Ventress in a failed effort to assassinate the CIS head of state.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Dathomir_Disciple.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180330034125) [![After Count Dooku carried out a genocide on Mahranee, the Jedi Council would dispatch Jedi Master Quinlan Voss alongside Dooku's former acolyte, Asajj Ventress in a failed effort to assassinate the CIS head of state.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Dathomir_Disciple.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180330034125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Dathomir_Disciple.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180330034125) 

After Count Dooku carried out a genocide on Mahranee, the Jedi Council would dispatch Jedi Master Quinlan Voss alongside Dooku's former acolyte, Asajj Ventress in a failed effort to assassinate the CIS head of state.

 

The Confederacy would attempt to commit a [mass genocide](/wiki/Atrocity_on_Mahranee "Atrocity on Mahranee") on the people of [Mahran](/wiki/Mahran "Mahran") under orders from Count Dooku. The planet was of strategic importance to the Confederacy because of its vast quantities of natural resources. In response, the people of Mahran begged the Jedi Council to send aid. The Jedi responded by sending Jedi General [Chubor](/wiki/Chubor "Chubor") with a task force of clone troopers. However, they were too late to prevent Separatist forces from laying waste much of the planet, including the [capital city](/wiki/Mahranee_capital_city "Mahranee capital city"). The Republic attempted to escort the remaining Mahranee off world but were stopped when the Separatists launched a massive attack, slaughtering all the civilians, Jedi and clones. After this massacre, Dooku attempted to lay the blame for the tragedy on the Jedi Council. This led the council to finally authorize an assassination attempt on the Count in a desperate bid to limit the war's casualties. The Jedi Council then sent [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") under the guise of a bounty hunter to recruit Asajj Ventress, who previously came close to killing Dooku and knew much about him, to aid him in the assassination. Their first attempt on Dooku ended in failure with Vos being captured, with a final plan to assassinate him during the [second battle](/wiki/Second_battle_of_Christophsis "Second battle of Christophsis") of Christophsis ending in[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) the apparent[[75]](#cite_note-TBB_article-75) death of his former apprentice Asajj Ventress.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

 [![Darth Sidous would have Dooku imprison the renegade Sith Lord Maul at a CIS prison on Stygeon Prime, though Maul would escape with the aide of his allies in Death Watch.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Maul_Guest_of_the_Spire.png/revision/latest?cb=20190128151605) [![Darth Sidous would have Dooku imprison the renegade Sith Lord Maul at a CIS prison on Stygeon Prime, though Maul would escape with the aide of his allies in Death Watch.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Maul_Guest_of_the_Spire.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190128151605)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Maul_Guest_of_the_Spire.png/revision/latest?cb=20190128151605) 

Darth Sidous would have Dooku imprison the renegade Sith Lord Maul at a CIS prison on Stygeon Prime, though Maul would escape with the aide of his allies in Death Watch.

 

Darth Sidious had brought [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") to the Spire, a prison fortress controlled by the Confederacy of Independent Systems on [Stygeon Prime](/wiki/Stygeon_Prime "Stygeon Prime"). It was there that Sidious briefly interrogated Maul, and told Count Dooku to find out information about who and where the Shadow Collective leaders were. The goal was to make Maul believe that the Sith wanted to destroy the [Shadow Collective](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective"), so he would seek out Mother Talzin. Meanwhile, Sidious was followed to Stygeon Prime by two Death Watch warriors, [Rook Kast](/wiki/Rook_Kast "Rook Kast") and [Gar Saxon](/wiki/Gar_Saxon "Gar Saxon"), under orders from Mandalore's Prime Minister, Almec to [free](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Spire "Escape from the Spire") Maul from the Spire.[[76]](#cite_note-SonOfDathomir1-76)

 [![Dooku dispatched General Grievous to wipe out Maul's forces on Zanbar, successfully forcing Maul to retreat to his criminal allies in the Shadow Collective.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Armies-on-Zanbar.png/revision/latest?cb=20231120150403) [![Dooku dispatched General Grievous to wipe out Maul's forces on Zanbar, successfully forcing Maul to retreat to his criminal allies in the Shadow Collective.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Armies-on-Zanbar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231120150403)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Armies-on-Zanbar.png/revision/latest?cb=20231120150403) 

Dooku dispatched General Grievous to wipe out Maul's forces on Zanbar, successfully forcing Maul to retreat to his criminal allies in the Shadow Collective.

 

After being freed, Maul was tracked to Zanbar by General Grievous along with a Separatist fleet. Dooku ordered Grievous not to kill Maul, simply to defeat and break his forces enough that Maul would seek out Mother Talzin's help. Grievous launched his forces towards the surface, and Maul's troops immediately began firing anti-aircraft weaponry at them. The heavy fire was not enough to repel the ships, however, so the Separatists pressed their [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Zanbar "Battle of Zanbar") and deployed all of their forces.[[76]](#cite_note-SonOfDathomir1-76) After the Shadow Collective lost on [Zanbar](/wiki/Zanbar "Zanbar"), Maul [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Ord_Mantell_(Yuuzhan_Vong_War) "Battle of Ord Mantell (Yuuzhan Vong War)") Dooku and Grievous over [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") which led Maul to make his way into orbit and boarded Grievous' command ship. Grievous disabled the battle droid army after Maul gave him the choice to do so or die, and the cyborg general was taken into custody. Dooku, meanwhile, had engaged and defeated the Nightbrothers in battle, before being captured by the Shadow Collective forces.[[77]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_2-77)

 [![CIS forces under Grievous continued to assault Maul's Shadow Collective, attempting to weaken the potential threat against Darth Sidous.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Battle_over_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest?cb=20190128043304) [![CIS forces under Grievous continued to assault Maul's Shadow Collective, attempting to weaken the potential threat against Darth Sidous.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Battle_over_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190128043304)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Battle_over_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest?cb=20190128043304) 

CIS forces under Grievous continued to assault Maul's Shadow Collective, attempting to weaken the potential threat against Darth Sidous.

 

Sidious and Grievous arrived to [confront](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Dathomir "Second Battle of Dathomir") Maul and Talzin on Dathomir after finding out where Dooku was being held, the latter of whom had used her [magick](/wiki/Magick "Magick") to take control of Dooku's body. This led to a [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") duel, in which Sidious quickly gained the upper hand against the Talzin-controlled Dooku. Talzin appeared in the flesh, returned to her physical form, and held off a [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") assault from Sidious and, eventually, Dooku. Talzin sacrificed her own life to allow Maul to escape, as Grievous fatally stabbed the Dathomirian witch through the chest while Maul fled from Dathomir. The Separatists, meanwhile, also attacked Maul's [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") and [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") allies, leading the [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") to end their alliance with Maul; destroying the Shadow Collective.[[78]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_4-78)

 [![The CIS would suffer a massive defeat against the Republic at Anaxes, with their entire invasion force being destroyed alongside famed CIS Admiral Trench.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Wrecker_happiest_moment.png/revision/latest?cb=20210622212459) [![The CIS would suffer a massive defeat against the Republic at Anaxes, with their entire invasion force being destroyed alongside famed CIS Admiral Trench.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Wrecker_happiest_moment.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210622212459)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Wrecker_happiest_moment.png/revision/latest?cb=20210622212459) 

The CIS would suffer a massive defeat against the Republic at Anaxes, with their entire invasion force being destroyed alongside famed CIS Admiral Trench.

 

The world of [Anaxes](/wiki/Anaxes "Anaxes") was [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Anaxes "Battle of Anaxes") by a Confederate [fleet](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet") under the command of Trench, starting the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges"), as the Separatists' last stand to force the Republic into surrender. He besieged the [Republic shipyards](/wiki/Anaxes_shipyards "Anaxes shipyards") for weeks on end, exploiting the Techno Union's access to a secret Republic strategy algorithm. Even as the tide of battle began to turn against him, Trench remained intent on annihilating the Jedi and their clone infantry. In a last ditch effort, he activated a bomb beneath the assembly complex on Anaxes. However, Anakin Skywalker infiltrated Trench's flagship and forced the admiral to divulge the sequence to disarm the device. When Trench tried to retaliate, Skywalker drove his lightsaber through his chest killing him and ending the battle.[[79]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-79)

#### The end of the war[]

##### Outer Rim Sieges[]

:   "*Looks like the Republic found the factory."  
    "They found nearly all of them. Drove us to the Outer Rim. It was the beginning of the end.*"
:   ―Gedeek Obaz and ND-5 talking about the Confederacy's loss of territory at the end of the war[[80]](#cite_note-Outlaws-80)

 [![The CIS faced the Republic in a battle at Mygeeto late in the war, as part of the Outer Rim Sieges.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Mygeetobridgebattle.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215035135) [![The CIS faced the Republic in a battle at Mygeeto late in the war, as part of the Outer Rim Sieges.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Mygeetobridgebattle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130215035135)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Mygeetobridgebattle.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215035135) 

The CIS faced the Republic in a battle at Mygeeto late in the war, as part of the Outer Rim Sieges.

 

By the last days of the Clone Wars, the Republic had pushed back the CIS, taking away most of its territory and effectively only leaving it with a few systems in the Outer Rim. To wipe out the Confederacy's last holdings,[[81]](#cite_note-CIS_history_gallery_10-81) the Republic was laying siege to the Confederacy in the Outer Rim and its holdings in other sectors, with battles taking place on [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Battle_of_Cato_Neimoidia "Battle of Cato Neimoidia"), [Mygeeto](/wiki/Fourth_Battle_of_Mygeeto "Fourth Battle of Mygeeto"), [Saleucami](/wiki/Siege_of_Saleucami "Siege of Saleucami"), [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), [Felucia](/wiki/Battle_of_Felucia_(Outer_Rim_Sieges) "Battle of Felucia (Outer Rim Sieges)"),[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) [Kaller](/wiki/Battle_of_Kaller "Battle of Kaller"), and [Lokori](/wiki/Battle_on_Lokori "Battle on Lokori")[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82)[[83]](#cite_note-The_Last_Padawan_1-83) while Grievous had launched an counter-offensive against the Republic, pushing its [military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") to the the breaking point. In response to the assault, [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") were deployed to help the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic").[[84]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-84) The Confederacy was also involved in a [confrontation](/wiki/Bracca_Invasion "Bracca Invasion") with the Republic on [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"), a planet in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"). The Confederacy intended to take control of the Republic world with the help of sympathizers of the [Scrapper Guild](/wiki/Scrapper_Guild "Scrapper Guild").[[85]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Jedi:_Fallen_Order-85)

 [![The CIS would launch a massive invasion of the Republic capital on Coruscant, though the battle would only end with the death of Count Dooku and the destruction of a large portion of the CIS fleet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Spacebattle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091019154628) [![The CIS would launch a massive invasion of the Republic capital on Coruscant, though the battle would only end with the death of Count Dooku and the destruction of a large portion of the CIS fleet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Spacebattle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091019154628)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Spacebattle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091019154628) 

The CIS would launch a massive invasion of the Republic capital on Coruscant, though the battle would only end with the death of Count Dooku and the destruction of a large portion of the CIS fleet.

 

The Separatists had launched a surprise [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") on the capital of the Galactic Republic, Coruscant and saw Chancellor Palpatine captured by Grievous and kept on board his command ship. However, this was a plan orchestrated by Sidious in order for Anakin to kill Dooku and replace him as Sidious's next apprentice, but no one was aware of the Sith Lords' true intention. The Republic sent General Kenobi and Master Skywalker to rescue the Chancellor. During their rescue attempt, they were confronted by Count Dooku and engaged him in a lightsaber duel. Dooku initially gained the upper hand, knocking Kenobi out, however, he was soon overpowered by Skywalker, who cut off his hands and then took Dooku's own lightsaber and held it to his throat along with his own, in a scissor position. At Skywalker's mercy, Dooku was betrayed by his master, as Palpatine ordered Anakin to kill him. Dooku was shocked and horrified, while likely also realizing that his own master used and betrayed him. Despite the fact that the count was an unarmed prisoner and that it was against the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code"), he was nevertheless beheaded by Skywalker. After rescuing the chancellor, they escaped to the bridge where Grievous lay in wait for them. They engaged him in a duel and managed to defeat him, but he managed to escape.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

 [![The Republic would launch an invasion of Utapau which resulted in the death of General Grievous.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Clone_Troops_Utapau.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210054331) [![The Republic would launch an invasion of Utapau which resulted in the death of General Grievous.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Clone_Troops_Utapau.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130210054331)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Clone_Troops_Utapau.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210054331) 

The Republic would launch an invasion of Utapau which resulted in the death of General Grievous.

 

Despite having lost a third of the attack fleet,[[86]](#cite_note-Bust_Collection_37-86) Grievous then ordered the fleet to withdraw and became head of state of the Confederacy of the Independent Systems, who fled to [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), which was [occupied](/wiki/Invasion_of_Utapau "Invasion of Utapau") by them[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) sometime after a [crystal incident](/wiki/Mission_to_Utapau "Mission to Utapau"),[[87]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-87) where he hid and met with the Separatist Council. After a brief disagreement with [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray"), he ordered both him, and the other confederate leaders to go to the [Mustafar system](/wiki/Mustafar_system "Mustafar system") for their safety. Shortly after arriving, his location was discovered by [Clone Intelligence](/wiki/Clone_Intelligence "Clone Intelligence"). This led the Jedi Council to send Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi to investigate. Having arrived in secret, Kenobi confirmed the presence of Grievous and ordered a [full-scale assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") on the settlement. During the ensuing battle, Grievous would be killed by Kenobi while trying to flee the sinkhole planet. Despite the survival of the Separatist Council,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) Grievous's demise marked the collapse of an effective command structure.[[88]](#cite_note-Aftermath-88)

##### Massacre on Mustafar[]

:   "*The war is over! Lord Sidious promised us peace. We only want—*"
:   ―Nute Gunray's last words, before being killed by Darth Vader — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/NuteGunraysLastWords.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403185135)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:NuteGunraysLastWords.flac "File:NuteGunraysLastWords.flac"))[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

 [![The Separatist leadership in hiding on Mustafar after the war ended.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/SeppyWarRoom-Ep3.png/revision/latest?cb=20130216061549) [![The Separatist leadership in hiding on Mustafar after the war ended.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/SeppyWarRoom-Ep3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130216061549)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/43/SeppyWarRoom-Ep3.png/revision/latest?cb=20130216061549) 

The Separatist leadership in hiding on Mustafar after the war ended.

 

Following this, the Galactic Republic [reformed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), with Palpatine declaring himself [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). On Mustafar, Darth Sidious conversed with the Separatist Council via [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram"), with Gunray remarking confidently that their plan had gone just as the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") had promised. Demoralized by their recent defeats, Gunray and the other leaders had wished to sue for peace, but did not know what Sidious had planned for them, who promised that his new apprentice would soon arrive to take care of them. Much to the councils' obliviousness, they were being double crossed by Sidious, who ordered Vader to eliminate them on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). Once Darth Vader landed, he entered the mining facility and slaughtered the Separatists, taking them out one by one with his [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber"); He also destroyed the [OOM-series security droids](/wiki/OOM-series_security_droid "OOM-series security droid"), an [OOM command battle droid](/wiki/OOM_command_battle_droid "OOM command battle droid"), multiple [Neimoidian](/wiki/Neimoidian "Neimoidian") [guards](/wiki/Neimoidian_Royal_Guard "Neimoidian Royal Guard"), and aides who had assembled in the room with their leaders.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

 [![Darth Vader would slaughter all members of the Separatist Council, resulting in the full collapse of the CIS command structure.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Mission-to-Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20210612085144) [![Darth Vader would slaughter all members of the Separatist Council, resulting in the full collapse of the CIS command structure.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Mission-to-Mustafar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210612085144)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Mission-to-Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20210612085144) 

Darth Vader would slaughter all members of the Separatist Council, resulting in the full collapse of the CIS command structure.

 

In rapid succession, Vader executed the Councilors,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) including [Po Nudo](/wiki/Po_Nudo "Po Nudo") of the planet [Ando](/wiki/Ando "Ando"),[[89]](#cite_note-Po_Nudo_Databank-89) [Passel Argente](/wiki/Passel_Argente "Passel Argente")[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) of the Corporate Alliance,[[90]](#cite_note-Passel_Argente_Databank-90) and [Presidente](/wiki/Presidente "Presidente") [Shu Mai](/wiki/Shu_Mai "Shu Mai") of the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild").[[91]](#cite_note-Shu_Mai_Shu_Mai-91) He then set his sights on [Tikkes](/wiki/Tikkes "Tikkes")[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) of Mon Cala, and Archduke Poggle the Lesser of Geonosis. Minister Wat Tambor of the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union"),[[43]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-43) who fled into a conference room, and [Rune Haako](/wiki/Rune_Haako "Rune Haako") of the Trade Federation were also soon killed. Begging for mercy, Nute Gunray was the final leader eliminated by Vader. After the slaughter, Vader received an order to send a transmission to the [Droid Control Ships](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_battleship "Lucrehulk-class battleship") of the Trade Federation to issue the immediate deactivation of all remaining droid units within the Separatist Droid Army. The signal[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) spread throughout the galaxy, such as on [Lokori](/wiki/Lokori "Lokori"), thus formally ending the war.[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82)

The ongoing [blockade of Quermia](/wiki/Blockade_of_Quermia "Blockade of Quermia") came to its end with the fall of the Separatists.[[36]](#cite_note-Savage_Spirits-36) With the Separatist Droid Army shut down,[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) the Empire had defeated the Confederacy, winning the Clone Wars[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) and bringing about the collapse of the CIS.[[5]](#cite_note-VE-5) While the various federations and guilds that held power under the CIS were crushed at that moment,[[92]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-92) many of the corporations would survive into the new era[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93) after they rushed to grovel before the Empire, pledging loyalty to the new regime and dropping their sponsorship of the defeated CIS. Without the sponsorship and financial aid of those corporations, combined with the loss of leadership and[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) the sudden shutdown[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) of the Droid Army, the Separatist cause quickly withered away. In particular, the usage of the Droid Army had allowed most Separatists to carry on with their lives without needing to learn to fight for themselves. As such, what remained of the Separatist military did not have the numbers to continue the fight, nor did they have the funding.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

 [![With the CIS in ruins and the Jedi Order destroyed, the Sith assumed full control of the Republic, with Darth Sidious becoming Emperor of the new Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/Proclamation-SWBC66.png/revision/latest?cb=20240221002458) [![With the CIS in ruins and the Jedi Order destroyed, the Sith assumed full control of the Republic, with Darth Sidious becoming Emperor of the new Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/Proclamation-SWBC66.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240221002458)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/Proclamation-SWBC66.png/revision/latest?cb=20240221002458) 

With the CIS in ruins and the Jedi Order destroyed, the Sith assumed full control of the Republic, with Darth Sidious becoming Emperor of the new Galactic Empire.

 

While some of the Confederate-loyal corporations would be absorbed into the Imperial government[[94]](#cite_note-CIS_DB-94) via nationalization,[[95]](#cite_note-Uprising-95) as occurred with the Trade Federation[[96]](#cite_note-BustCollection13-96) and Techno Union[[95]](#cite_note-Uprising-95) despite the efforts of both to appease the Empire,[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) many,[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93) such as the Corporate Alliance,[[97]](#cite_note-Stealth_Strike-97) Commerce Guild, and Banking Clan, were permitted to remain active[[98]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Conspiracy-98) thanks to their quick pledges of loyalty.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) In the case of the Banking Clan in specific, the Empire controlled the group[[99]](#cite_note-Crimson_Climb-99) after the Republic had claimed its banks during the war,[[74]](#cite_note-Crisis_Heart-74) yet the Imperials would allow the organization a degree of flexibility.[[99]](#cite_note-Crimson_Climb-99)

### Legacy[]

#### Reintegration into the Empire[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist Reintegration Day](/wiki/Separatist_Reintegration_Day "Separatist Reintegration Day")

:   "*Dooku was right in the end. He knew the Republic was corrupt, that it would collapse and become something worse. He saw it coming. The Galactic Empire.*"
:   ―Governor of Desix Tawni Ames[[100]](#cite_note-Solitary_Clone-100)

 [![Former Separatist worlds were reintegrated into the new Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/OccupationofRaxus-CG.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111040120) [![Former Separatist worlds were reintegrated into the new Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/OccupationofRaxus-CG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220111040120)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/OccupationofRaxus-CG.png/revision/latest?cb=20220111040120) 

Former Separatist worlds were reintegrated into the new Galactic Empire.

 

Immediately after the war, [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") led a [celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order](/wiki/Celebration_marking_the_eradication_of_the_Jedi_Order "Celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order") on Coruscant and claimed to the crowd that the Jedi had been behind the "Separatist plots" that had threatened them.[[101]](#cite_note-The_Chosen_One_1-101) Sweeping into the former Confederacy's territory[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93) and taking advantage of the unprepared Separatist citizenry, who had not been ready to fight the Empire themselves thanks to their reliance on the corporations and Droid Army,[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) the Empire proclaimed it was not the Confederacy's enemy, claiming their regime would treat all planets within the CIS fairly in exchange for their loyalty.[[102]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-102) In reality, however, all former Separatists would come to suffer under Imperial rule.[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93) Indeed, members of the Separatist Senate were arrested, and the capital of Raxus was [occupied](/wiki/Occupation_of_Raxus "Occupation of Raxus") by the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military").[[102]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-102)

 [![A city on Serenno was destroyed by the Empire via orbital bombardment.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Serenno_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20230114135402) [![A city on Serenno was destroyed by the Empire via orbital bombardment.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Serenno_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20230114135402)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Serenno_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20230114135402) 

A city on Serenno was destroyed by the Empire via orbital bombardment.

 

With the Confederacy's robotic armies withdrawn[[103]](#cite_note-TBotCW-103) or outright defeated,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Imperial_Army "Imperial Army") was able to march through former Separatist territory[[102]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-102) without fear of a military resistance.[[103]](#cite_note-TBotCW-103) The Empire swiftly conquered and [occupied](/wiki/Occupation_of_Serenno "Occupation of Serenno") [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno"). with at least [one](/wiki/Serenno_City "Serenno City") of the planet's cities, in view of [Castle Serenno](/wiki/Castle_Serenno "Castle Serenno"), destroyed via [orbital bombardment](/wiki/Orbital_bombardment "Orbital bombardment").[[26]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-26) Quermia was finally liberated from the Confederacy's massive blockade with the government's fall but quickly fell under Imperial rule.[[36]](#cite_note-Savage_Spirits-36)

 [![On worlds like Desix, local Separatist holdouts desperately attempted to resist Imperial control, only to be eventually wiped out by the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Mission_to_Desix.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230125085531) [![On worlds like Desix, local Separatist holdouts desperately attempted to resist Imperial control, only to be eventually wiped out by the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Mission_to_Desix.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20230125085531)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Mission_to_Desix.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230125085531) 

On worlds like Desix, local Separatist holdouts desperately attempted to resist Imperial control, only to be eventually wiped out by the Empire.

 

Seeking to make examples of worlds who continued to harbor secessionist tendencies, worlds like [Kooriva](/wiki/Kooriva "Kooriva"), [Murkhana](/wiki/Murkhana "Murkhana"), and [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"), the formal capital of the Confederacy, which still hosted ex-Separatists, became targets of the Empire. One such example, assigned to [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") Wilhuff Tarkin, was on the once-loyal Separatist moon, [Antar 4](/wiki/Antar_4 "Antar 4"). During the [genocidal atrocities](/wiki/Antar_Atrocity "Antar Atrocity") committed on the moon's population, Imperial forces made no attempt to sort the Separatists from the Imperial loyalists. This served to compel Raxus and other worlds to surrender all former Separatists to Imperial custody, or else suffer a similar demise to that of Antar 4.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

#### Last remains[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts")

:   "*The Jedi betrayal ended the war for most of the galaxy. But here on Agamar, I assumed it was a Republic trick and prevented the shutdown command.*"
:   ―Kalani[[104]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-104)

 [![The early Imperial Navy spent much of its time hunting down Separatist holdouts across the galaxy, with the Empire often using the continued existence of these holdouts as an excuse to advance their military technology.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/Imperialattackcruisers.png/revision/latest?cb=20140317112248) [![The early Imperial Navy spent much of its time hunting down Separatist holdouts across the galaxy, with the Empire often using the continued existence of these holdouts as an excuse to advance their military technology.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/Imperialattackcruisers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140317112248)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/Imperialattackcruisers.png/revision/latest?cb=20140317112248) 

The early Imperial Navy spent much of its time hunting down Separatist holdouts across the galaxy, with the Empire often using the continued existence of these holdouts as an excuse to advance their military technology.

 

The end of the Clone Wars was not acknowledged by all elements of the Confederacy, with some possibly not being unaware it was over,[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) as the former Confederacy was absorbed into the fledgling Galactic Empire whose [Navy](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") began to root out the remaining surviving [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts") who had not surrendered and stopped fighting for at least four years after the Clone Wars.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

 [![Due to the sheer size of the Separatist Droid Army, scattered remnants would persist across the galaxy, with Imperial protocol in place to destroy any active CIS battle droids when encountered.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Battle_droid_squad_six.png/revision/latest?cb=20210902014934) [![Due to the sheer size of the Separatist Droid Army, scattered remnants would persist across the galaxy, with Imperial protocol in place to destroy any active CIS battle droids when encountered.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Battle_droid_squad_six.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20210902014934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Battle_droid_squad_six.png/revision/latest?cb=20210902014934) 

Due to the sheer size of the Separatist Droid Army, scattered remnants would persist across the galaxy, with Imperial protocol in place to destroy any active CIS battle droids when encountered.

 

The super tactical droid General Kalani, who assumed that the order was instead a Republic trick, and prevented the deactivation[[104]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-104) of his large [garrison](/wiki/Agamar_garrison "Agamar garrison")[[105]](#cite_note-USWNE-105) of droids marooned on Agamar in the wreckage of a [DH-Omni Support Vessel](/wiki/Unidentified_DH-Omni_Support_Vessel_(Agamar) "Unidentified DH-Omni Support Vessel (Agamar)")[[104]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-104) that had crashed during a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Agamar_(Clone_Wars) "Battle of Agamar (Clone Wars)") fought on the planet,[[106]](#cite_note-Build_R2_51-106) where they would await retrieval during the next seventeen years.[[107]](#cite_note-2_BBY-107) Kalani's remaining forces consisted mostly of [B1-series battle droids](/wiki/B1-series_battle_droid "B1-series battle droid") and a few [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka"), though they lacked any heavy vehicles or starships capable of leaving the planet. The munitions depot they were protecting at the base kept Kalani and his droids well-provisioned enough to still remain reasonably functional for almost two decades without resupply.[[104]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-104)

 [![Imperial military leaders Wilhuff Tarkin and Hurst Romodi were placed in command of the Empire's war against Separatist holdouts, successfully pacifying hundreds of former CIS worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Tarkin_Scarif.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106061908) [![Imperial military leaders Wilhuff Tarkin and Hurst Romodi were placed in command of the Empire's war against Separatist holdouts, successfully pacifying hundreds of former CIS worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Tarkin_Scarif.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20170106061908)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Tarkin_Scarif.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106061908) 

Imperial military leaders Wilhuff Tarkin and Hurst Romodi were placed in command of the Empire's war against Separatist holdouts, successfully pacifying hundreds of former CIS worlds.

 

By the early [Imperial period](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"),[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) remnants of the Confederacy of Independent Systems had fled into the [Western Reaches](/wiki/Western_Reaches "Western Reaches").[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) Various planetary populations of former Confederate worlds were dissatisfied with the lack of reconstructive action in the aftermath of the Clone Wars, joining the holdouts and thus swelling their numbers in their [campaign](/wiki/Pacification_operations_in_the_Western_Reaches "Pacification operations in the Western Reaches") against the Empire[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) that lasted until until [17 BBY](/wiki/17_BBY "17 BBY").[[108]](#cite_note-17_End_Date-108) Imperial [shipyards](/wiki/Shipyard "Shipyard") like the one in orbit over [Kartoosh](/wiki/Kartoosh "Kartoosh"), just outside of the Western Reaches, served as a repair hub for [starships](/wiki/Starship "Starship") damaged in engagements with Separatists as well as [salvage yards](/wiki/Salvage_yard "Salvage yard") for captured vessels.[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82) The [Bilbringi shipyards](/wiki/Bilbringi_shipyards "Bilbringi shipyards") also served as a dismantling point for old Separatist warships. The Imperial forces were led by Tarkin, fresh from "pacifying Antar 4," who had been assigned to oversee operations by Emperor Sheev Palpatine himself.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) Both Tarkin and [Lieutenant Commander](/wiki/Lieutenant_Commander "Lieutenant Commander") [Orson Krennic](/wiki/Orson_Callan_Krennic "Orson Callan Krennic") would utilize the conflict against the holdouts as a pretext to justify for the appropriation of numerous [legacy worlds](/wiki/Legacy_world "Legacy world")—worlds legally protected as ecological reserves—advancing the top-secret Imperial [construction project](/wiki/Project_Stardust "Project Stardust") occurring above Geonosis.[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82)

 [![Many former CIS leaders, such as General Kleeve, would find themselves on the run to avoid Imperial retribution.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Kleeve-Kanan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180128070345) [![Many former CIS leaders, such as General Kleeve, would find themselves on the run to avoid Imperial retribution.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Kleeve-Kanan1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20180128070345)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Kleeve-Kanan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180128070345) 

Many former CIS leaders, such as General Kleeve, would find themselves on the run to avoid Imperial retribution.

 

After the war, some Separatists took on lives that operated outside of the law; the prestigious General [Kleeve](/wiki/Kleeve "Kleeve") took on the name "Jondo" and worked off the planet [Lahn](/wiki/Lahn "Lahn").[[109]](#cite_note-Kanan_4-109) In addition, the enterprising Imperial Navy officer [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") collected Separatist weapons and technology, including a [buzz droid](/wiki/Pistoeka_sabotage_droid "Pistoeka sabotage droid").[[110]](#cite_note-Thrawn-110) By [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"),[[111]](#cite_note-5_BBY_Date-111) former Separatists were still among the rebels groups who defied the Empire.[[112]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-112) One such Separatist, [Anto Kreegyr](/wiki/Anto_Kreegyr "Anto Kreegyr"),[[113]](#cite_note-Narkina_5_Story_Gallery-113) was one of [Luthen Rael](/wiki/Luthen_Rael "Luthen Rael")'s [contacts](/wiki/Axis_network "Axis network").[[112]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-112)

#### Remembrance[]

:   "*If the contagion of separatism ever gets loose again it will infect the entire galaxy, not just one world.*"
:   ―[Beck Ollet](/wiki/Beck_Ollet "Beck Ollet")[[114]](#cite_note-Edge_of_the_Galaxy-114)

 [![The Galactic Empire completed the Geonosian-designed Death Star, intending to use the space station to enforce fear.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TarkinDeathStar-RogueOne.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161231002913) [![The Galactic Empire completed the Geonosian-designed Death Star, intending to use the space station to enforce fear.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TarkinDeathStar-RogueOne.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161231002913)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TarkinDeathStar-RogueOne.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161231002913) 

The Galactic Empire completed the Geonosian-designed Death Star, intending to use the space station to enforce fear.

 

Separatist military equipment (including battle droids) that survived the war was used by a number of pirate and resistance organizations, including [Berch Teller](/wiki/Berch_Teller "Berch Teller")'s [rebel cell](/wiki/Berch_Teller%27s_rebel_cell "Berch Teller's rebel cell")[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) and the insurgent leader [Nevil Cygni](/wiki/Nevil_Cygni "Nevil Cygni").[[110]](#cite_note-Thrawn-110) A large amount of heavily modified Separatist equipment was used by the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"); examples include the [IG-227 *Hailfire*-class droid tank](/wiki/IG-227_Hailfire-class_droid_tank "IG-227 Hailfire-class droid tank"), the *Lucrehulk*-class Battleship, and the [Armored Assault Tank](/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank_Mk_I "Armored Assault Tank Mk I").[[115]](#cite_note-SWC-115) The [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") pilot [Temmin Wexley](/wiki/Temmin_Wexley "Temmin Wexley")'s best friend was a former B1 battle droid named [Mister Bones](/wiki/Mister_Bones "Mister Bones").[[116]](#cite_note-Aftermath_novel-116) Criminal organizations composed of re-purposed battle droids such as the [Droid Gotra](/wiki/Droid_Gotra "Droid Gotra") operated in Imperial Center's underground, while some escaped notice all together.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) The destruction of many of the corporations that had allied with the Separatists opened a power vacuum, allowing smaller groups to step in; the [Fardi clan](/wiki/Fardi_clan "Fardi clan") took advantage of the opening, using it to rise into power without allying with large crime families.[[92]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-92)

 [![In spite of Imperial propaganda, a Rebel Alliance would emerge to challenge their control of the galaxy, with some former CIS vehicles and warships being deployed by the rebellion against the Imperial war machine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/BattleOfTingelDeepspaceBesh-EGTW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120302003029) [![In spite of Imperial propaganda, a Rebel Alliance would emerge to challenge their control of the galaxy, with some former CIS vehicles and warships being deployed by the rebellion against the Imperial war machine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/BattleOfTingelDeepspaceBesh-EGTW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120302003029)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/BattleOfTingelDeepspaceBesh-EGTW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120302003029) 

In spite of Imperial propaganda, a Rebel Alliance would emerge to challenge their control of the galaxy, with some former CIS vehicles and warships being deployed by the rebellion against the Imperial war machine.

 

During the Age of the Empire, the tale of the Clone Wars was frequently used as a warning to the galaxy of what could happen should the Empire and order fail.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) Soon after the Empire's formation, Emperor Palpatine and Darth Vader observed the construction of the Death Star, a super-weapon which had begun construction shortly after the Second Battle of Geonosis by the Separatists. With the Separatists defeated and their leaders killed, the Death Star project was taken over by the Galactic Empire, who planned to use it to control the galaxy.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) Nineteen years later, the Death Star was used to [destroy](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") the planet [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), killing all the inhabitants. The Death Star was later destroyed during the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") when a young Rebel pilot, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), exploited a serious design flaw to destroy the battle station, making the battle a major Rebel victory in the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War").[[117]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-117)

An aging veteran of the Clone Wars,[[118]](#cite_note-Alphabet_Squadron-118) [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Shakara Nuress](/wiki/Shakara_Nuress "Shakara Nuress") continued to see her enemies as Separatists, referring to the Alliance by the name, much to the amusement of her younger crew.[[119]](#cite_note-TIE_Fighter_1-119) After the Alliance to Restore the Republic was re-organized into the New Republic after it won the war, it was decided that the capital of the New Republic would be rotated periodically—addressing one of the main concerns of the Confederate systems.[[120]](#cite_note-TFAVD-120)

#### Resurgence[]

:   "*Give up? I never give up. I didn't give up the corrupt Republic, I didn't give up to the Empire, and I won't give up to you."*  
    *"You're a Separatist?"*  
    *"Separatist is a pejorative term. I support democracy. Count Dooku was a visionary. He was cut short in his prime by the Jedi enforcer…*"
:   ―Helgait and Bo-Katan Kryze[[121]](#cite_note-Chapter_22-121)

By the final year of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), the Separatist movement was given a new lease of life.[[17]](#cite_note-AEE-17) In [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"),[[16]](#cite_note-Empire's_End_date-16) a new and ambitious[[122]](#cite_note-Battles-122) galactic government[[17]](#cite_note-AEE-17) known as the [New Separatist Union](/wiki/New_Separatist_Union "New Separatist Union") had taken shape in the territories where the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic")'s control was only theoretical.[[122]](#cite_note-Battles-122) In 5 ABY,[[123]](#cite_note-VPdate-123) several border skirmishes [broke out](/wiki/Border_skirmishes_with_the_New_Separatist_Union "Border skirmishes with the New Separatist Union") between the two factions.[[124]](#cite_note-Victory's_Price-124) By the closing days of the Galactic Civil War, [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma") herself had become increasingly unsettled by the rise to power of the New Separatist Union, as well as the rise of the [Confederacy of Corporate Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Corporate_Systems "Confederacy of Corporate Systems") and the pirate-led [Sovereign Latitudes of Maracavanya](/wiki/Sovereign_Latitudes_of_Maracavanya "Sovereign Latitudes of Maracavanya").[[17]](#cite_note-AEE-17)

Having lived through the fall of both the Republic and Empire, the elderly Separatist named [Helgait](/wiki/Helgait "Helgait"), despite his years of loyal service to the [royal family of Plazir-15](/wiki/Royal_family_of_Plazir-15 "Royal family of Plazir-15"), began a campaign of terror across the independent planet [Plazir-15](/wiki/Plazir-15 "Plazir-15") in his capacity as [commissioner](/wiki/Commissioner "Commissioner") of the Plazir-15 Security Office after [Plazir-15's duchess](/wiki/The_Duchess "The Duchess") married the former Imperial [Bombardier](/wiki/Bombardier_(individual) "Bombardier (individual)"). Exploiting the world's reliance on droids, including former Separatist battle droids, by spiking their [Nepenthé](/wiki/Nepenth%C3%A9 "Nepenthé") [lubricant](/wiki/Lubricant "Lubricant") with [nano-droids](/wiki/NM-K_reconstitutor "NM-K reconstitutor"), Helgait's reprogrammed droids created chaos across Plazir-15 until the Mandalorians [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin") and [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze") uncovered and apprehended him. Before his arrest, Helgait revealed his Separatist loyalties, heralding the late Count Dooku as a visionary who was struck down in his prime.[[121]](#cite_note-Chapter_22-121)

## Organization[]

### Government[]

:   "*In accordance with the Bylaws of Independent Systems, a voice vote is required.*"
:   ―Dooku[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1)

 [![Dooku acted as Head of State of the CIS, but, in secret, was following the plans laid out by his Sith Master](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923030000) [![Dooku acted as Head of State of the CIS, but, in secret, was following the plans laid out by his Sith Master](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120923030000)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923030000) 

Dooku acted as Head of State of the CIS, but, in secret, was following the plans laid out by his Sith Master

 

A union of independent governments and thousands of star systems, the Confederacy of Independent Systems was a confederate government organized and directed by former Jedi Master, Count Dooku,[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) who served as the government's Head of State throughout much of the Confederacy's duration.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) Acting through the [Bylaws of Independent Systems](/wiki/Bylaws_of_Independent_Systems "Bylaws of Independent Systems"), an established constitution that vested capabilities to the Confederacy's parliament, Dooku operated as an officiator within the legislature for congressional procedures.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) In theory,[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125) the CIS was thus a democracy with Dooku simply as its executive figure and senatorial leader. In practice, however, Dooku secretly held great power over the state[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) and was granted even greater authority over it as the Clone Wars dragged on.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) He manipulated its senate[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125) and the overall state to meet the ends of the Sith. Instead of actually answering to the will of the people,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) Dooku answered only to Sidious, who, as Dooku's Sith Master, alone could order the count.[[54]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-54) To meet his ends, Dooku manipulated the senate.[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125)

Disparagingly referred to as "the Separatists" by those within the Galactic Republic, the Confederacy's ideological beliefs centered around minimal taxation and trade regulations, as it provided its member systems with an increase in control over their territories. Furthermore, the confederate government also offered assurances to its allies of a smaller and less centralized government, as well as freedom for local governments in order to privately maintain their internal affairs, while also offering egalitarian representation for governments that were left isolated within the galaxy's Rim regions from the Core Worlds and Republic Senate.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2)

 [![The Separatist Senate on Raxus was overseen by Dooku and filled by representatives of Separatist member worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TheAyesHaveIt-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518044104) [![The Separatist Senate on Raxus was overseen by Dooku and filled by representatives of Separatist member worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TheAyesHaveIt-HOBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130518044104)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TheAyesHaveIt-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518044104) 

The Separatist Senate on Raxus was overseen by Dooku and filled by representatives of Separatist member worlds.

 

Although its system of government appealed to multiple intellectuals and self-styled "free-thinkers," those of whom were inhabitants of the regions beyond the core, the Confederacy developed and came against two extensive issues. Firstly, as the Republic was militarily opposed to the secessionist movement, the CIS government's members worlds were required to relinquish control and resources to Dooku and the Executive Separatist Council in order to maintain their war effort.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) In practice, such control allowed Dooku to exert great power over the state.[[126]](#cite_note-Crisis-126) Furthermore, Dooku and his officers—such as General Grievous[[127]](#cite_note-Massacre-127)—were free to use the CIS military to commit massacres without answering to the senate. Dooku's political supporters were left unaware and believed in the image of a humanitarian leader who acted in their best interest.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) While covered up by Dooku, who would deny such practices if asked about them, the Confederacy also made use of torture.[[59]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-59)

The second major problem faced by those who aligned with the Separatists came from the confederate government's laissez-faire stance in response to star systems' rights. Such a stance resulted in many Republic protections for workers, such as antislavery laws, autochthonous sentients' rights, and environmental exploitation and protection laws, being rendered ineffective. Unable to control their whole destiny and faced with a lack of those protections, localized resistances would emerge on numerous worlds out of dissatisfaction with the realities of separatism.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) One Separatist fighter, [Soujen Vak-Nhalis](/wiki/Soujen_Vak-Nhalis "Soujen Vak-Nhalis"), found himself forced to admit that the Confederacy had made a terrible deal in signing itself over to corporate masters. To true Separatist believers like himself, such was done in the name that Separatist worlds might have a chance at self-determination by winning the war, with Vak-Nhalis hoping greatly that the deal would prove wise in the end.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

 [![The corporate leaders of the Separatist Council on Utapau shortly after the Battle of Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/SepCouncilUtapau-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20141122180512) [![The corporate leaders of the Separatist Council on Utapau shortly after the Battle of Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/SepCouncilUtapau-ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20141122180512)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/SepCouncilUtapau-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20141122180512) 

The corporate leaders of the Separatist Council on Utapau shortly after the Battle of Coruscant.

 

With the Clone Wars, Dooku was provided wartime powers by the Separatist Parliament that undermined its democratic values.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) Indeed, despite the ideals of his Separatist supporters,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) the CIS in practice was a state that saw Dooku able to implement executive orders in regards to governmental decisions, resulting in the undermining of the democratic process and making the parliament ineffective.[[126]](#cite_note-Crisis-126) The position of Head of State also granted the state leader direct power over the Separatist Council,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) an executive advisory and administrative body formed from the leaders of the major galactic corporations that supported the Confederacy, such as Trade Federation Viceroy Nute Gunray, Federation Settlement Officer Rune Haako, Techno Union Foreman Wat Tambor, Commerce Guild Presidente Shu Mai, InterGalactic Banking Clan Chairman San Hill, Corporate Alliance Magistrate Passel Argente, Senators [Po Nudo](/wiki/Po_Nudo "Po Nudo"), [Tikkes](/wiki/Tikkes "Tikkes") and [Rogwa Wodrata](/wiki/Rogwa_Wodrata "Rogwa Wodrata"), and Geonosian Archduke Poggle the Lesser.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2)

The Separatist Council managed much of the Confederacy alongside Dooku. Furthermore, it was also responsible for the oversight of the government's daily operations and vital planetary occupations, as well as additional situations that were related to its efforts in the Clone Wars.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) Much like the Separatist Senate,[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125) however, the council would find itself virtually powerless under Dooku's leadership. Instead, the group was to follow the will of the count and his Sith Master.[[128]](#cite_note-CIS_history_7-128) Still, while Dooku needed to keep his Sith loyalties a secret from the Separatist Senate,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) the Separatist Council was more than aware of the existence of Darth Sidious and the Sith Order's control over the Separatist state.
