However, the council did not know that the entire Separatist government was to be destroyed at war's end.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) Unlike Dooku, who acted for the betterment of the Sith Plan,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) council members worked in the name of the Confederacy[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) or for their own profit in the case of corporate members like Gunray[[129]](#cite_note-Cargo_of_Doom-129) and Tambor.[[130]](#cite_note-On_the_Wings-130) In the end, the Separatist Council was another group that was manipulated by the Sith and sacrificed for Sidious's greater goals.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

 [![Grievous succeeded Dooku as the Head of State but remained subservient to Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grievous-speaks-to-Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20230211014302) [![Grievous succeeded Dooku as the Head of State but remained subservient to Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grievous-speaks-to-Sidious.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230211014302)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grievous-speaks-to-Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20230211014302) 

Grievous succeeded Dooku as the Head of State but remained subservient to Darth Sidious.

 

Following Dooku's death in the Confederacy's assault on the Republic capital world of Coruscant,[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) control over the confederate government,[[4]](#cite_note-Front_Lines-4) its military forces[[122]](#cite_note-Battles-122) and protection of the Separatist Council was vested to the cybernetic warlord General Grievous, who had served as the [Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies](/wiki/Supreme_Martial_Commander_of_the_Separatist_Droid_Armies "Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies") throughout the war's duration. A position held for only several days after Dooku's death, Grievous was silenced not long after his appointment to Head of State,[[4]](#cite_note-Front_Lines-4) which thereby transferred overall control of the Confederacy to a demoralized Separatist Council.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

### Politics[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate")

:   "*I'm not sure there was a* right *side. I opposed the Separatist Confederacy because it chose violence when other paths remained. It seemed to me—it still seems to me—that its cruel tactics and disregard for life were inseparable from the greed that drove the Confederacy's corporate elite. I also acknowledge that many well-meaning people saw matters differently and opposed the Republic for good and moral reasons. I've come to wonder if the whole war was a sort of feint—half a misdirection on the part of those who desired an Empire. Palpatine and his cronies pushed and pushed until the fighting started. Count Dooku was a… The particulars don't matter. But by joining the war, all of us played into Palpatine's hands.*"
:   ―Bail Organa, to Soujen Vak-Nhalis[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

Headquartered on the Confederacy's capital world of Raxus Secundus, the Separatist Senate was a legislative body of senators that governed the confederate government, while also existing primarily for mutual defense and dispute mediation. Independent from the obsolete mandates and proprieties that bridle the Republic coupled with corruption, the parliament lightly directed the Confederacy under the supervision of [Separatist Congress Leader](/wiki/Separatist_Congress_Leader "Separatist Congress Leader") and Speaker, Senator Bec Lawise.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) However, despite serving as the government's legislature, the Separatist Parliament was granted with minimal power in practice:[[31]](#cite_note-Collapse_of_the_Republic-31) despite the ideals of its members,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) the senate operated in practice only as an advisory body to Dooku and the Executive Separatist Council,[[31]](#cite_note-Collapse_of_the_Republic-31) which handled the government's funding and military-based matters.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) Even then, there were moments where the senate surprised Dooku. In such cases, such as[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125) Senator Mina Bonteri's proposed peace accord with the Republic,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) Dooku worked to undermine the actions of his own people.[[125]](#cite_note-CIS_history_8-125)

 [![The Separatist Senate was housed on Raxus.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/SeparatistSenate-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518043828) [![The Separatist Senate was housed on Raxus.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/SeparatistSenate-HOBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130518043828)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/SeparatistSenate-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518043828) 

The Separatist Senate was housed on Raxus.

 

Separatist senators were all from worlds and systems who joined the Separatist cause, including ones that had once been members of the Galactic Senate that continued to represent their constituents in the Confederacy, and had involvement in public affairs. The senate was seated on the Confederate capital planet of Raxus Secundus. Many loyalists and senators of the Republic believed that the Separatist senators were no more than pawns to Dooku. Furthermore, the senators of the parliament as well as the citizens of the Confederacy were repeatedly shielded from front-line reports of brutal campaigns waged by the Separatist Droid Army by the various elements of the Separatist hierarchy.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1)

Representing the civilians of the Confederacy,[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) the Separatist Parliament was responsible for coordinating the mutual defense and mediating disputes between its members. It delegated most of its authority on taxation and trade regulation to its member systems, in accordance with the decentralized ideology of the Confederacy.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) All the while, however, the vast majority of power in the Separatist government was claimed by the Executive Council and military, robbing the parliament of its potential to make change. There were many in the Separatist Senate who desired secession without war, yet they believed the Republic had failed to listen to their pleas and they had no other choice.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) While the worst of the Confederacy's war crimes were hidden from its populous,[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) many senators were aware that certain "excesses" were undertaken by the military. Many in the senate opposed those "excesses"[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) without knowing the extent of the problem.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

### Defense[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Confederacy military](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military"), [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), [Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems_Navy "Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy"), [CIS Special Operations](/wiki/CIS_Special_Operations "CIS Special Operations") and [Separatist Intelligence](/wiki/Separatist_Intelligence "Separatist Intelligence")

:   "*Our friends from the Trade Federation have pledged their support. And when their battle droids are combined with yours, we shall have an army greater than any in the galaxy. The Jedi will be overwhelmed. The Republic will agree to any demands we make.*"
:   ―Count Dooku to the Separatist leadership[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![General Grievous leads the Droid Army in battle.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest?cb=20230529060353) [![General Grievous leads the Droid Army in battle.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230529060353)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Clone-War-battlefront.png/revision/latest?cb=20230529060353) 

General Grievous leads the Droid Army in battle.

 

The various commercial entities who joined under the banner of the Confederacy of Independent Systems pledged their forces to the [military](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military"), creating one sprawling group of droids as well as organic forces, and local warriors, and was often referred to as the Droid Army, and was headed by a Supreme Commander.[[6]](#cite_note-Character_Encyclopedia-6) These units were led by organic [officers](/wiki/Separatist_officer "Separatist officer")[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) as well as [tactical droids](/wiki/Tactical_droid "Tactical droid") to lead ground and naval forces, which included of the [T-series tactical droid](/wiki/T-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "T-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid")[[131]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-131) and the more sophisticated super tactical droid.[[132]](#cite_note-DB-132) The Confederacy's droid army was the largest droid ground force in history.[[133]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_21-133)

The Separatist war effort was focused upon economics and volume, as exemplified by its deployment of mass-produced, expendable battle droids in overwhelming numbers.[[134]](#cite_note-DesigningTwilight-134) The droid army was composed from the Trade Federation's battle droids to the security forces maintained by the Commerce Guild, InterGalactic Banking Clan, and Corporate Alliance, which donated not only its new [B2-series super battle droids](/wiki/B2-series_super_battle_droid "B2-series super battle droid"), but numerous foundries capable of producing thousands more droids for deployment as well as the [OG-9 homing spider droids](/wiki/OG-9_homing_spider_droid "OG-9 homing spider droid") were a common sight on many front lines, and [tank droids](/wiki/NR-N99_Persuader-class_droid_enforcer "NR-N99 Persuader-class droid enforcer") and AATs provided heavy firepower.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)[[135]](#cite_note-WW-135) while also consisting of local forces of the worlds under its control,[[61]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-61)[[64]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-64)[[136]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-136)[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) who were of flesh and [blood](/wiki/Blood "Blood"), however, government officials downplay this and stated that they were volunteers and not like the Republic [cloned](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") soldiers which had been pressed into service.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

 [![Naval warships active as part of the Confederacy's fleet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Separatist-frigates-Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20210727222528) [![Naval warships active as part of the Confederacy's fleet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Separatist-frigates-Ryloth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210727222528)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Separatist-frigates-Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20210727222528) 

Naval warships active as part of the Confederacy's fleet.

 

Its [naval wing](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems_Navy "Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy") was originally made up of heavily armed [bulk transports](/wiki/Bulk_transport "Bulk transport") from Separatist member corporations, but, as the Clone Wars continued, [Pammant Docks](/wiki/Pammant_Docks "Pammant Docks") and other Separatist allies built [capital ships](/wiki/Capital_ship "Capital ship") to make a creditable fleet. These [starships](/wiki/Starship "Starship") were filled with a variety of [starfighters](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") and crewed by B1 battle droids,[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) within it fleet, it included the *Subjugator*-class heavy cruiser[[43]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-43) which had [mega-ion cannons](/wiki/Mega-ion_cannon "Mega-ion cannon") that could disable the power systems of entire fleets, rendering them defenseless against the ship's massive array of [lasers](/wiki/Laser "Laser").[[45]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-45)

### Outside relations[]

:   "*Say it aloud before this gathering—as representative for Chancellor Palpatine that* you *declare, without reservation, the Separatist state* legitimate*.*"
:   ―Senator Voe Atell to delegations from the Galactic Republic during a rare [conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference") on Mandalore[[38]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-38)

When the Confederacy of Independent Systems was formed, it received limited galactic recognition from many other entities due to a lack of legitimacy from the Galactic Republic as a separate state, but they did receive secret support from several major galactic corporations.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) [Intergalactic Association of Amalgamated Droid Builders](/wiki/Intergalactic_Association_of_Amalgamated_Droid_Builders "Intergalactic Association of Amalgamated Droid Builders") was also aligned with the Confederacy, providing construction and service for the Separatists' Droid Army.[[28]](#cite_note-Propaganda-28) On the surface,[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) the Confederacy was not interested in "conquering" the Republic; instead, its supporters wanted a chance at self-determination[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) and many were open to existing alongside the Republic[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) after making the war too costly for the Republic to proceed[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) or finding a form of peace with their rival government.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) While the Separatists believed the Republic may collapse under its own contradictions given time, the war was only a way to secure their own future.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) However, the true face of the Confederacy—expressed through its military wing[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93) and hidden from its general population[[137]](#cite_note-Mina_SWE-137)—sought the destruction of the Republic.[[93]](#cite_note-SW_Book-93)

 [![The representatives of the Republic and the Confederacy meeting on Mandalore in an effort to end the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) [![The representatives of the Republic and the Confederacy meeting on Mandalore in an effort to end the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/274?cb=20121211041358)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) 

The representatives of the Republic and the Confederacy meeting on Mandalore in an effort to end the Clone Wars.

 

The [New Mandalorians](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians") government,[[37]](#cite_note-TMP-37) stayed neutral during the pan-galaxy conflict, and decided to agree to allow Mandalore as neutral ground to host an historic [peace conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference") between representatives of the Republic and the Confederacy in an effort to end the Clone Wars, where the separatists sought full diplomatic recognition from the Republic, which it did not grant,[[38]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-38) a recurring issue since its birth as a separate state,[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) but negotiations talks would result in failure.[[38]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-38)

The Confederacy moved to [annex](/wiki/Annexation_of_the_Qiilura_system "Annexation of the Qiilura system") the [Qiilura system](/wiki/Qiilura_system "Qiilura system") during the Clone War.[[138]](#cite_note-MM-138) Later, they entered into relations with the [Grysk Hegemony](/wiki/Grysk_Hegemony "Grysk Hegemony"), a warlike species hailing from the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") who had maintained surveillance on the Confederacy prior contact, they then decided to share information on [cortosis](/wiki/Cortosis "Cortosis"), which was resistant against lightsabers.[[139]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-139)

With the Confederacy keeping close ties with certain criminal groups and mercenaries,[[140]](#cite_note-Lawless_Pirates-140) several groups of [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") also signed terms with the Confederacy of Independent Systems to exclusively target the Galactic Republic during the Clone Wars, these were the [Delmaasi](/wiki/Delmaasi_pirates "Delmaasi pirates"), [Iridium](/wiki/Iridium_Pirates "Iridium Pirates"), [Nuro](/wiki/Nuro_pirates "Nuro pirates"), [Red Fury Brotherhood](/wiki/Red_Fury_Brotherhood "Red Fury Brotherhood"), [Merson](/wiki/Merson_pirates "Merson pirates") and [Nuala Marauders](/wiki/Nuala_Marauders "Nuala Marauders") pirates, who were encouraged by Count Dooku to harass Republic supply lines.[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) As a result of the Separatist alliance with such groups, their technology occasionally ended up in the possession of pirates or other such groups.[[140]](#cite_note-Lawless_Pirates-140)

## Society and culture[]

:   "*I can only wonder what Count Dooku offered Vallt's new leadership. Perhaps he promised to tug this world a bit closer to your star."  
    "Trade, respect, fair representation in the Confederacy. All that we weren't receiving as a member of the Republic.*"
:   ―Galen Erso and [Gruppe](/wiki/Gruppe "Gruppe")[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82)

 [![The Confederacy of Independent Systems was primarily made up of  and .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/SeparatistSenate3-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518043946) [![The Confederacy of Independent Systems was primarily made up of  and .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/SeparatistSenate3-HOBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130518043946)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/SeparatistSenate3-HOBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518043946) 

The Confederacy of Independent Systems was primarily made up of [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") and [near-humans](/wiki/Near-human "Near-human").

 

The Confederacy of Independent Systems population consisted of several different non-[human](/wiki/Human "Human")[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") groups,[[110]](#cite_note-Thrawn-110) as well as [near-humans](/wiki/Near-human "Near-human"),[[141]](#cite_note-AotG-141)[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) this being reflected in both its military and political as it hierarchy was largely dominated by non-humans. All species were seeking for fair trade, respect, and better representation in the Confederacy.[[31]](#cite_note-Collapse_of_the_Republic-31)[[82]](#cite_note-Catalyst-82)[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14) Despite its many alien supporters,[[110]](#cite_note-Thrawn-110) humans could occupy high ranking roles within the Confederacy, such as its head of state, Count Dooku, being a [Serennian](/wiki/Serennian "Serennian"),[[139]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-139) as well as [Onderonian](/wiki/Onderonian "Onderonian") King [Sanjay Rash](/wiki/Sanjay_Rash "Sanjay Rash")[[66]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-66) and senator Mina Bonteri.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) Having been ignored by the Republic, most of the [Alvadorjian](/wiki/Alvadorjian "Alvadorjian") clans sided with the CIS on the promise that it could provide a future for their dwindling species.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

Separatist believers prided their politics off the idea that, while the Republic[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) and its Supreme Chancellor had become pawns of corporate monopolies,[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) the CIS was free to stand as a real democracy. While the CIS did business with major corporations, its members believed they were not ruled by these factions.[[1]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-1) However, in practice, the great power given to these corporate actors through their representation on the Executive Separatist Council[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) and as the state's sponsors left the government at their mercy. As Soujen Vak-Nhalis was forced to admit, the corporations, at the end of the day, had become his masters. Vak-Nhalis defended the alliance with these self-interested corporate actors as a necessary evil—even if, by his own admission, the deal in practice had been horrible for Separatists like himself—because they uplifted and gave the Separatists who already wanted to leave the Republic the ability to fight. Continuing to fight despite the realities of life under these corporations, Separatists like Vak-Nhalis hoped they might, through victory, have a chance at self-determination.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

During the Battle of Mon Cala, the Separatists exploited tensions between the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") and Quarren by backing the latter.[[135]](#cite_note-WW-135) Count Dooku also ordered the [enslavement](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") of Mon Calamari prisoners and civilians.[[142]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-142) Despite supporting the Quarren, Dooku made a secret agreement with the [Karkarodon](/wiki/Karkarodon "Karkarodon") leader [Riff Tamson](/wiki/Riff_Tamson "Riff Tamson") to crown him the new King of Mon Cala.[[58]](#cite_note-Prisoners-58) The Confederacy later committed genocide against the Mahran species and attacked their homeworld, killing many civilians and [refugees](/wiki/Refugee "Refugee"). In addition, the Confederacy also issued an order that all Mahrans were to be regarded as extremely hostile and killed on sight.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

 [![A Separatist propaganda poster named .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Fighting_for_Your_Independence.png/revision/latest?cb=20201011181240) [![A Separatist propaganda poster named .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Fighting_for_Your_Independence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201011181240)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Fighting_for_Your_Independence.png/revision/latest?cb=20201011181240) 

A Separatist propaganda poster named *[Fighting for Your Independence](/wiki/Fighting_for_Your_Independence "Fighting for Your Independence")*.

 

According to Dooku's propaganda, the Galactic Republic and the Jedi Order were the victims of their own ambitions. He also alleged that the Supreme Chancellor was the pawn of corporate monopolies and that the Jedi had secretly created the Grand Army of the Republic to suppress the Confederacy's demands for reforms and equality. While the Republic's clone troopers were regarded as unwilling slaves who were regularly sent to their deaths, the Separatists sacrificed mainly droids. Dooku also claimed that the Confederacy's flesh and blood soldiers were willing participants who were fighting for freedom.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

Count Dooku was the main leader of the Confederacy of Independent Systems who served as a unifying force in the Separatist State. Many Separatists viewed him as a single, seemingly invincible figurehead to rally around. Some observers like the Jedi Master Mace Windu believed that eliminating Dooku would lead to the disintegration of the Separatist movement. To boost morale, Dooku traveled to several worlds including Raxus where he gave rousing speeches defending the Confederacy's cause and war effort. Wherever he traveled, Dooku was greeted by large crowds. Unaware of atrocities like the Attack on Mahranee[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) or General Grievous's campaigns,[[137]](#cite_note-Mina_SWE-137) Dooku was respected enough within the Confederacy to be conferred with awards like the [Raxian Humanitarian Award](/wiki/Raxian_Humanitarian_Award "Raxian Humanitarian Award").[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18)

## Infrastructure[]

:   "*Yes, Count Dooku succeeded in using the HoloNet for Separatist propaganda purposes, but Republic forces were quick to shut down those Shadowfeeds.*"
:   ―[Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Dodd Rancit](/wiki/Dodd_Rancit "Dodd Rancit") to [Harus Ison](/wiki/Harus_Ison "Harus Ison"), regarding Dooku's Shadowfeeds during the Clone Wars[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13)

The Separatist State gained a vast transportation network as systems and sectors broke away from the Republic during the Separatist Crisis which served as means of both civilian and military transport to support its objectives. This included several major hyperspace lanes—which were considered trans-galactic highways—with their knowledge and existence dating back to well before the Galactic Republic. Their control was vital for maintaining an effective means of defense and security during the Clone Wars.[[18]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-18) The Confederacy needed to throw the majority of its resources into the war against the Republic. For that reason, the CIS had no time to try and discover new hyperspace routes by charting and mapping them out.[[143]](#cite_note-Insider228-143)

The Confederacy made use of the unauthorized [holofeed](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet") network known as the [Shadowfeeds](/wiki/Shadowfeed "Shadowfeed") to spread [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") into Republic Space on the order of Count Dooku[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) and to provide news and entertainment to its own citizens.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) Shadowfeeds were created through sabotage of legitimate HoloNet networks[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) and established as their own network by the CIS.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) While [Republic Intelligence](/wiki/Republic_Intelligence "Republic Intelligence") was able to shut down many of these Shadowfeeds quickly, which eventually led to the creation of the [Commission for the Protection of the Republic](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Protection_of_the_Republic "Commission for the Protection of the Republic"),[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) the network itself managed to survive and even persisted into the Imperial Era, enabling the usage of Shadowfeeds among surviving Separatists,[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12) other anti-Imperial actors,[[144]](#cite_note-sketch-144) and criminal elements.[[145]](#cite_note-Dawn_1-145) The governor of the planet Eriadu, Wilhuff Tarkin, was responsible for frustrating Dooku by providing counterintelligence to shut down many of his Shadowfeeds during the Clone Wars.[[13]](#cite_note-Tarkin-13) "[The Factory](/wiki/The_Factory "The Factory")" was a media outlet that provided propaganda content for the Shadowfeeds ranging from entertainment to creditable takedowns of Republic personnel.[[12]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-12)

## Astrography[]

### Expansion and growth[]

:   "*As I explained to you earlier, I am* quite *convinced that ten thousand* more *systems will rally to our cause.*"
:   ―Dooku, to the Separatist Council — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Dooku-Rally-AOTC.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403184725)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Dooku-Rally-AOTC.flac "File:Dooku-Rally-AOTC.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

The Confederacy of Independent Systems numbered at several thousand [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system"), that had left the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") at the [start](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"),[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) which were [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet") primarily from the [Inner](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") to [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"),[[116]](#cite_note-Aftermath_novel-116) including the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") world of [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"), among others,[[146]](#cite_note-Databank_Raxus-146) such as [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"),[[147]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Geonosis-147) and [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar").[[148]](#cite_note-Databank_Mustafar-148) The spice-producing world of [Nooroyo](/wiki/Nooroyo "Nooroyo") fell within Separatist space during the Clone Wars.[[35]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-35) The [Deep Core](/wiki/Deep_Core "Deep Core") planet [Empress Teta](/wiki/Empress_Teta "Empress Teta") also joined the Confederacy.[[149]](#cite_note-Nexus-149)

Several neutral and unaligned worlds also were annexed by the Confederacy as the war dragged on, [such](/wiki/Battle_of_Dathomir "Battle of Dathomir") as [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"),[[150]](#cite_note-Bounty-150) and [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum "Florrum").[[151]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-151) As noticed by Ahsoka Tano, populations on worlds occupied by the Separatist Alliance would at first closely follow every new rule put in place. However, they also made sure to see what reaction occurred when these directives were violated. Afterward, the local population would begin to push back against the occupiers, doing an extreme pushback if the Separatists were violent in their reaction.[[92]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-92)

### Falling back and wars end[]

The Confederacy was pushed back to the spiral arms of the galaxy during the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges") in the third and final [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") as the Republic continued to keep the pressure in these territories,[[152]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-152) continuing to take place until the final [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") of the Clone Wars.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_III-14)

## Behind the scenes[]

### Development[]

The Confederacy of Independent Systems first appeared in [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) Early in production of *Attack of the Clones*, the various commerce guilds were to all employ the same type of battle droids that were used by the Trade Federation, albeit with different color schemes to differentiate allegiance, but it was later decided that having each guild have their own wholly unique droids would provide visual diversity.[[153]](#cite_note-Dwarf_Spider_Droid_Original_DB-153)

### Historical comparisons and analysis[]

The book *[Star Wars and History](/wiki/Star_Wars_and_History "Star Wars and History")* compared the establishment of the "Separatist Confederacy" and its declaration of civil war to the [Confederate States of America](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Confederate_States_of_America "wikipedia:Confederate States of America") seen in American history. The book suggests that the election of new leaders, Palpatine in the case of the Republic and [Abraham Lincoln](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abraham_Lincoln "wikipedia:Abraham Lincoln") in the case of the American government, were the spark that created the respective separatist crises. The authors then note they do not seek to compare Lincoln to the fictional villain that is Palpatine, instead raising the connection to claim a change in upper leadership helped lead to war in both cases.[[154]](#cite_note-SW_and_History-154)

Author [Jason Fry](/wiki/Jason_Fry "Jason Fry") also pulled from the American Civil War when crafting lore about the Republic harnessing its industrial power for the war against the Confederacy, taking the idea from the Union's industrial and manpower advantage over the CSA.[[155]](#cite_note-Fry_Nonfictional-155) While the CIS canonically outnumbered the Republic in military manpower thanks to its formations of battle droids,[[104]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-104) its population was smaller,[[156]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-156) and the Droid Army had taken heavy losses by the war's end anyway.[[157]](#cite_note-Aftermath_EP-157) Furthermore, the Republic indeed managed to outpace the Separatists in industrial manufacturing by the end of the war,[[122]](#cite_note-Battles-122) by which point the Confederacy was also losing much of its territory and thus was even more heavily outnumbered in a territorial sense.[[152]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-152) All the same, in a blow to any "heroic" narrative around industrial production that could be applied to the Clone Wars,[[158]](#cite_note-Paul_Tweet_1-158)[[159]](#cite_note-Paul_Tweet_2-159) the Republic's harnessed industrial might set up the military industrial complex that remained under the Galactic Empire.[[122]](#cite_note-Battles-122)

### Contradictions[]

The [German-exclusive novelization](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(German_novelization) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (German novelization)") of[[160]](#cite_note-German-160) the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019")[[161]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-161) audio play *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* contains an erroneous mention of the Separatists long before[[160]](#cite_note-German-160) the CIS would ever be formed. While the Separatist Alliance was established[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) in [24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY "24 BBY")[[11]](#cite_note-Formation_date_note-11) by the former Jedi Dooku,[[2]](#cite_note-Rise-2) the novelization sees the Separatists mentioned as a force already active when Dooku is still a member of the Jedi Order. In the text, Dooku is depicted as an enemy of the Separatists, who are described as a rebel and, in Dooku's eyes, criminal movement that hide in the vastness of the—as described by the text—largely isolated Outer Rim Territories, only leaving to strike out against the Republic with terrorist attacks, such as the explosion of a cerium refinery on Mandalai. Typical targets of the Separatists are Republic defense personnel and the government's trade routes. Dooku—who regards the Separatists as a despicable force—involuntarily thinks of and blames the Separatists when he hears an explosion in a crowd.[[160]](#cite_note-German-160)

The *Dooku: Jedi Lost* German novelization was published on [September 20](/wiki/September_20 "September 20"), 2021,[[162]](#cite_note-Penguin-162) but, according to [Lucasfilm Story Group](/wiki/Lucasfilm_Story_Group "Lucasfilm Story Group") member [Leland Chee](/wiki/Leland_Chee "Leland Chee"), likely never saw any kind of review by their team as he was unfamiliar with the book until being told of its existence by fans.[[163]](#cite_note-Novel_Review-163) There is no such mention of the Separatists during Dooku's days as a Jedi in the widely released audio drama[[161]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-161) nor its [script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)").[[164]](#cite_note-JediLostscript-164) As such, this article disregards this information.

[↑](#cite_ref-Retail_Caucus_Droid_10-0) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Retail Caucus Droid](https://www.starwars.com/databank/retail-caucus-droid) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20190910055139/https://www.starwars.com/databank/retail-caucus-droid)) 11. ↑ [11.0](#cite_ref-Formation_date_note_11-0) [11.1](#cite_ref-Formation_date_note_11-1) [11.2](#cite_ref-Formation_date_note_11-2) *[Rise of the Separatists](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Separatists "Rise of the Separatists")* establishes that the [Raxus Address](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address") and following foundation of the Confederacy of Independent Systems occurred two [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). Therefore, CIS was formed in [24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY "24 BBY"). Additionally, because the ratification of the [Geonosian accord](/wiki/Geonosian_accord "Geonosian accord") first appeared in *Attack of the Clones*, the events of which are dated to 22 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") by *Timelines*, the accord must have been ratified in 22 BBY. 12. ↑ [12.00](#cite_ref-Mask_of_Fear_12-0) [↑](#cite_ref-Galactic_Atlas_15-0) *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* 16. ↑ [16.0](#cite_ref-Empire's_End_date_16-0) [16.1](#cite_ref-Empire's_End_date_16-1) According to *[Aftermath: Empire's End](/wiki/Aftermath:_Empire%27s_End "Aftermath: Empire's End")*, [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma") was worried about the rise of the New Separatist Union [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") before the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku"). Since *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates that battle to [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"), the New Separatist Union must have been formed by that [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"). 17. ↑ [17.0](#cite_ref-AEE_17-0) [17.1](#cite_ref-AEE_17-1) [17.2](#cite_ref-AEE_17-2) [17.3](#cite_ref-AEE_17-3) *[Aftermath: Empire's End](/wiki/Aftermath:_Empire%27s_End "Aftermath: Empire's End")* 18. ↑ [18.00](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-0) [18.01](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-1) [18.02](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-2) [18.03](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-3) [18.04](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-4) [18.05](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-5) [18.06](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-6) [18.07](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-7) [18.08](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-8) [18.09](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-9) [18.10](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-10) [18.11](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-11) [18.12](#cite_ref-Dark_Disciple_18-12) *[Dark Disciple](/wiki/Dark_Disciple "Dark Disciple")* 19. [↑](#cite_ref-Fry_Nonfictional_155-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Jason Fry](/wiki/Jason_Fry "Jason Fry") ([@jasoncfry](https://twitter.com/jasoncfry)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/jasoncfry/status/1755689246348726636)): "It is indeed. Pretty much a straight steal from the US fighting a nonfictional Confederacy. (In response to: "The heroic narrative of industrial production to me echoes a recurring theme in American history where the US side wins through industrial might & population -the North having more factories & men than the South, we had the ability to fight Japan & Germany in WW2 simultaneously because America's insane industrial might could equip a massive two front war, etc. I tagged both of you since citing both authors made the most sense, but if you say this was Jason's contribution I wonder if this theme is what he was drawing on")" ([backup link](https://archive.is/bjvim)) 156.
